Geluwa
Wolayttatto doonan Toophphiya bila xifatiya woshettaa giyo korssee Wolayttatto doonan luxiya luxanchchatussi Wolaytta doonaa bilaa/ bila xifatiya guyye dendduwa gidiya taarikiyaanne eta xaafi kessida asatu maaduwa akeekissanaassa. Ha korssiyan luxanchchati Toophphiya bila xifatiya Wolayttatto doonaara gattidi wochchiyogaanikka wudidi  xanna’ana.   Hegaa gishshawu  dumma dumma xaafanchchatun xaafettida dumma dumma maxaafata loytti nabbabidi kase de’iya eraara gattidi aahuwan akeekana bessees. Luxanchchati Toophphiya bila xifatiya xeelliyagan puttu giida dumma dumma xaafanchchata eti xaafido maxaafaa  huuphe yohuwaaranne cuccumaara gattidi shaakkidi erana.qassikka dummatettan wolayttatto bila xifatiyaa /doonaa bilaa xeelliyagankka kasetiya amarida xaafanchchata eti xaafidobas huuphe yohuwaara gattidi shaakkana. Ingglizettonne Amaaratto Toophphiya bila xifatiya xeelliyagan xaafettida dummabata dummabata  loytti wudidi erana.  Ingglizetto Toophphiya bila xifatiya qommota shaakkidi issuwa issuwa  eranaageekka luxanchchatuppe naagettees. 
Ha korssiyan muleera  ichchashu shemppoti de’oosona. Etakka kasiya kaaluwan wottiyo wode ha kaalliyagaadan uttidosona. Koyro shemppoy Ingglizettuwan Toophphiya bila xifatiya, Inggilizetto Toophphiya bila xifatiyawu guyye dendduwa, Toophphiya bila xifatiyawu Geerata (xinxxiso qofata), Ithioppikke woykko Gi’ize bila xifatiya, Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya bila xifatiya qommota h.h. milatiyageeta bari garssan oyqqees. Naa”antto shemppoy Toophphiya bila xifatiyan Wolayttatto doonaa  bila xifatiya woshettaa,Wolaytta deriya denddo / guyye woykko hayddaa, Wolaytta giya sunttay bessiyobaa, Wolaytta biittaa qantta qonccissuwa,  wolaytta biittan beettiya erettida zannaqqa sohota,Wolaytta dere deretettaa, wogaa,wolaytta kattaanne ushshaa qommota, wolaytta maayuwa qommuwa, wolaytta asaa ammanuwa h.h. milatiyageeta gatti oyqqes.  Heezzantto shemppoy Wolaytta xaafo bilaa woshettaa  gididi  wolaytta xaafo bilaa woshettaa maaduwa, wolaytta xaafo bilaa shaakkiyo ogeta h.h. milatiyageeta  bari garssan oyqqees.  Oyddantto shemppoy Wolaytta xaafettida doonaa bilaa/bila xifatiya-wolaytta chii medhdhi xaafuwa aybatettaa, chii- medhdhi xaafo gidida maxaafaa qommota, wolaytta medhdhi xaafuwa aybatettaanne giigissuwa,medhdhi xaafuwa ufurettaa h.h.milatyageeta. Ichchashantto shemppoy    Wolaytta attamettidanne attamettibeenna  bila xifatiya/doonaa bilaa oosota, Wolayttan kasetiya  doonaa bilaa xiftiya xaafancchatanne eta oosota haraatakka   bari garssan oyqqees. 


                      KOYRO SHEMPPUWA
1. INGGLIZETTUWAN TOOPHPHIYA BILA XIFATIYA
Tamaaretoo, ha shemppuwan, Afirkkaa bila xifatiya shaaho gidiya Toophphiya bila xifatiya Inggilizettuwan  tobbana.  Qassikka  xaaxi waaxo anotiya Toophphiya bila xifatiya hanotaabaanne  Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya bila xifatiya dummayidi xeellana.
Ha shemppuwa sintta qofata	
Ha shemppuwa wurssi simmidi luxanchchati:-
?	Toophphiya bila xifatiya xaaxi waaxuwan birshshananne qonccissana.
?	Toophphiya bila xifatiya qaaxettaa Inggilizettuwaaninne ano bila xifatiya oosuwa Toophphiya bila xifatiya oosuwa Inggilizettuwan oottida asata akeekana 
?	Inggilizettuwan beettiya Toophphiya bila xifatiya ano cuccumata shaakkana.
?	Toophphiya xaafanchchatun Ingglizetto doonan xaafettida bila xifatiya birshshananne nashshana
?	Toophphiya xaafanchchati bantta bila xifatiya oosotun go’ettido  Inggilizetto doonaa paaccana.
?	Toophphiya bila xifatiyaaninne Afirkkaa billa xifatiya garssan de’iya issipetettaanne dummatettaa xeellana
?	Toophphiya Diyasppora bila xifatiya xaaxi waaxo misiliya akeekana
1.1.	Inggilizettuwan  Toophphiya bila xifatiyawu guyye dendduwa
Meeziya -1
Kaalliya oyshatussi citan gidi tobbidi zaaruwa immite
Toophphiya bila xifatiya giyogee woygiyogee? Qonccissidi xaafite
__________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2.Toophphiya bila xifatiya birshshiyoode nuuni qoppana bessiyo allaalleti aybee aybee?
__________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
1.1.1. Toophphiya bila xifatiyawu Geerata (xinxxiso qofata)
Toophphiya bila xifatiya birshshanawu nookkanaappe kasetidi Afirkkaa bila xifatiya birshshettaa xeelliyoogee lo”o. Afirkkaa bila xifatiya birshshettawu wuday wogaa,xeelaa,polotikaa,xifatiya biittaawatettaanne  bila xifatiya doonaa.  Xaaxi waaxin Afirkkaa bila xifatiyan bila xifatiya/doonaa bila oosota eranawu Afirkkaa asatu de’uwa hayyuwa eranawu, Afirkkaa otta pilggettaa (philosophy), Afirkkaa wogaa,Afirkkaa polotikaa,Afirkkaa issippetettaa allaalleta phoolissana koshshees. Yohuwan qassi xaafanchchay Afirkkaa asa woyko Afirkka asa gidennan aggana danddayees. Hegaadankka Toophphiya bila xifatiya birshshiyoode, nuuni ha ubba allaalleta qoppana koshshees.
Toophphiya bila xifatee/doonaa bilay doonan haasayettidanne Toophphiyan wogan, xeelan,hayyuwaaninne oyddantto xeetu layttaappe doommidi hanno gakkanaashin Toophphiya doonatuuninne Inggilizetto doonan de’iya polotikaa bila xifate. Hagee beni wode bila xifate oosota, leemisuwaassi;Akisume kawotettaa wode oyddantto xeetu layttaa Gi’ize bila xifatiya tookkiis.
Meeziya-2
Ane   waattan waattan gididi garssaara imettida oyshata zaarite 
1.Toophphiya bila xifatee/doonaa bilay awudenne  ay mala hanotan doommidee ? 
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2.Toophphee  kiristtinnaa ammanuwa awude ekkidee? He wode oosettidabati aybee aybee?
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
3. Ubba deretettaa shaahotuppe daro xeetu layttatussi Toophphiyaassi tamaarida cora asay de’anaadan oottidabay aybee? Qonccissite.
____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
1.1.2. Ithiyoppikke woykko Gi’ize bila xifatiya
Toophphiya bila xifatee naa’u sha’u layttatuppe kasiyan shuchchaa bollan molidi xaafido xuufetun doommiis. Ha doonay qassi kiristtinnaa ammanoy oyddantto xeetu layttan he moottan erettiyoode woykko he moottaakko geliyoode bila xifatiyawu simmidi keehin koshshiya miishsha gidida  Ithiyoppikke( woykko Gi’ize) doonaakko dicciis. Hagee betiyaageeti Tohossa shaaho Arebe peninsula (ha’i wode  Yemenenen) Yesuus kirsttoosappe kasiyan issi sha’u ( millennium) layttan shuchchaa bollan molidi xaafido xuufeta Huuphessa Toophphiyan aggiyo wodee assi doometta. Cora sheeshshati Tohossa Arebeeppe Toophphiya doonaa dummayidi medhdhanawunne dumma pitalee, Ithiyooppikkee woykko Gi’izee, koyruwan guttumattu kanchchiya oyqqidi, simmidi ustta malaatatuura guttuma anuwaakko gujjiyoogan walahettidosona. Ha ooratta doonaanne ooratta pitaliya dichchay Toophphiyaassi keehin cora go’aa immiyoogaadan qonccettiis.
Toophphiya oyddantto xeetu layttan  Toophee kiristtinaa ammanuwa ekkiyoode, he wodiyan Geeshsha maxaafaa, tuma milatiya taarikiya (apocrypha) maxaafatuura gujjin birshshetta oosoy doommiis. Ha maxaafatuppe amaridaageeti, leemisuwaassi, Heenooka maxaafay kumettan Toophehe kanchchiyan de’iyaanne  zammaana birshshettati  appe gididosona.Ha oosoti mataara hara ammanotuuninne ayyaanaama timirttiya bila xifatiyan kaaletettidosona. Naa”anttoogaappe  corati  Haymaanoote Abewu ( aawatu ammanuwa) garssan shiiqidosona.  Toophphiyaassi qassi dummatiya woosa keettaa maara mankkati, geeshshatu de’oti (dariya baggi kare biittaa asatinne amarida Toophephe asati)nne, woosa maxaafati hagee qassi orddidi beettiya Toophphiya kiristtinnaa ammanuwa  eeshsha gidiyaagee de’ees.Ha wodiyankka Woosa keettay ammaniyaageeta tamaarissanawunne qeeseta loohissanawu timirtte keettaa/luxetta golliya doommiis.Ha timirtte hiillay qassi ubba deretettaa shaahotuppe daro xeetu layttatussi Toophphiyaassi tamaarida cora asay de’anaadan oottiis.Timirttee woosa keettaa eqotatun Toophphiya asati muleera giyo maladan ay guyyiyaappekka deretettaa giddon xoqqa sohotukko diccanaadan oottiis. Mataarakka, xaafanchchatu koshshay hara allaalleta giddo gelissanawu, eeqa maxaafata gujjin( leemisuwaassi, Biirannaa/scroll/ nne kitaabaa) nne mereta alamiya (“bestiary” woykko fisilagos giyoogee ayyaanaama timirtteti dumma dumma do’atu qonccissuwaappe yiyo maxaafa.Maxaafati otta pilggettaa( philosophy) shooqan harinne haraashin naa’u maxaafati etassi amarida palanttiyaabay( phalqqettay) de’iyoogeeti murutidosona.Toophphiyan tumu zammaana bori nashshiya otta pilggettay Awurooppan doommido wodiyan doommiis. Wogaa woykko higgiya maxaafatikka de’oosona. Fitha Negest(kawotu wogay) laatamaantto xeetu layttaa naa”antto baggaa gakkanaashin baaso Toophphiya woga woykko higge.Taarikkiyan kawotu kirinookilee ( chronocle) murutiis. Wurssettan dumma (classical) geetettida Toophphiyan merettida danttoy/( poetry) Gi’iziyaanne Amaarattuwa ba garssan oyqqiis.
Gi’ize bila xifatiyaassi  Amaarattoy Gi’iziya sohuwa haasaya doonadan ekkiyo wode  gita ciiyettay giddo layttatun de’ees. 14tto xeetu layttaa kasiyaappe 20tto xeetu layttaa gakkanaashin Kawotu kirinokile  meran  me’enna Toophphiya taariketu sanssalatay de’ees.He wodiyan kaalettiyaageetun zuppeto maaday de’ikkonne aadhdhidanne  ha’iba gidiya Toophphiyaabaa erissiya (akeekissiya) daro gita maaduwa immiis.
Medhdhi eko oosoy 14tto xeetu layttaappe, kawotu bonchchuwa (The Glory of Kings) Isra’eele kawuwa Solomonabaa  tumu taarikedan yootanawu milatissiyoogan Toophphiya wogan woykko meeziyan dumma sohoy de’ees. Hegaadankka Saaba kaweenne Toophphiyan 1270-1274, hegeekka doona taarikiyan(ledgend) odettiyoogaadan yesuusappe kasiyan 1000 laytta heeraa guyye biya Toophphiyan kawotida Solomona kawotettaa baasidaagaa geetettiya na’aa Minilike I (koyruwaassikka)  Toophphiya wogan dumma sohoy de’ees. Kawotu turaassinne misile bilaassi daro yesuwa denttettida taarikiyaassi gidiya woppaa immidaagee kawotu chartteriya. 
Hara baggaara qassi, Toophphiya bila xifatiyan Teodros Kiroosi xaaxi waaxuwan qonccissidoogaadan Toophphiya bila xifatee Inggilizetuwan dummatidi ha kaalliyaagaadan uttees. 
Toophphiya bila xifatee heezzu aaho kifiliyawu shaahettees:  hegaappe Kilaasikale (classical) bila xifatiya taarike odota, goobaa danttuwa woykko wolddayinnuwnne (poetry) baappe medhdhiyo meran molettida ootta pilggettaa phoolisso oosota, siiqonne (romantic) bila xifatiya Amaarattuwaaninne naa”antto Alame olaappe doommin ooratta Inggilizetto bila xifatiya xaaxi waaxi ba garssan oyqqees.  Kilaasiikaale bila xifatee ba dumma qaala xaafettaara naa”u sha’u layttaa heeran gal”a xaafattida Afirkkaa doona gidiya Seemanttikke  doonaa gi’iziyan qonccettees. Geeshsha maxaafaynne hara ubba kirsttinnaa ammanuwa  maxaafati Gi’iziyawu birshshettidosona.  Gi’izee ha’i wodiyan Toophphiya qeesetu doona gididi de’ees. Hagaa mala hanotan Gi’iziyawu arggo alamiyan laatiniyaagaara issimala xekkay de’ees. Toophphiyan coo asati gi’iziyan  haasayibookkonanne xaafibookkona.
Hegaa gishshawu he doonan xaafettida maxaafati dere asaa shemppuwaassi aybanne xokissibookkonanne Toophphiya bila xifatiya wogaa woykko meeziya murutissibookkona. Kilaasiikkaale bila xifatiya maxaafati, Ayyaanaama yettatinne eedoti ha’i wodiyan beettiyoy qeeseta gidiyaageetu achchaaninne Gi’iziyan keehin dummayidi loohida tamaaretunne  asttamaaretu achchaana. Hagee uddufuntta xeetu layttaa wurssettan purida Amaaratto doonan erettida Toophphiya xaaxi waaxiya wogaa kaalettanawu halchchidi ooratta doonaa zammaana Toophphiya haaro biittatun kaalettanawu de’iya gaasotuppe issuwa.  
Meeziya-3
 Kaalliya  oyshata citan gididi tobbite
1. Amaarattoy   koyro kochhooro O wodiyan beettidaakko ereetii? 
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2. Amaarattoy xaafo doonadan minnidoy O wodiyaanee?
____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
3. Amaarattoy  koyruwan awan xaafettidi awan attamettidee?
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
1.1.3. Zammaana Amaaratto Bila Xifatiya
Hanno gakkanaashin shiiqiiddi de’iya haasayettida hayyo xaafo bilaappe (oral literature)  haray Amaarattuwaassi haydaa oosotun xaafettiya doonadan doomettidobay de’ees.   Hara baggaara qassi Amaarattuwa go’ettiyo koshshay maataa Akisumeppe Lasttakko woykko Solomona Woybetuwaappe( dynasty) Zaaguwe woybetuwawu laammi simmin oosuwan pee’idaba gidikkonne, koyruwan Amaarattoy Amide Tsiona wodiyan beettiis. Qassikka Amaaratto doonay xaafo doonadan  minnidoy kawotu kawuwa Tewodiroosa wodiyaana. Amarida dookimentteti bessiyooaadan kawotu kawuwa Tewodiroosa kironookiletuppe amarida shaahoy Aleqaa/gadaawaa/ Zenneben Amaarattuwan xaafettiis. Yohuwan qassi 1908an koyro Amaaratto adussa medhdhi xaafoy Naples giyoosan xaafettidi Romen attamettiis. Hegawu gaasoy Xaaliya eranchchati he doonaa xanna’anawu maxaafaa  koyyido gishshataassa. Tobbiya LebbWallad Taariki ( meeze qaalan  “[Taarikee] Wozanaa yeletaa”) Afiworq Gebiren( 1868-1947) xaafettidaagee ha wodiyan keehin erettidaagaa. Hagee Amaarattuwan xaafettida adussa medhdhi xaafuwa  yuussaa erissees. Gebiree ha adussa medhdhi xaafuwan kiristtinnaa ammanuwaaninne Isilaama ammanuwa giddon zaari zaari yiya  karssi karssaa akeekees.Yoonaasa Adimaasu xeellidoogaadan, ha baaso adussa medhdhi xaafoy  koyro  beetuwan haysiya kawushshanawu (simplicity) nunan kum”u giis.  Gidikkonne A kawushsha hayse giidi shaakkanaagee meto, ubbakka bala. Oosoy shaahuwa kanttiyo ayibinne  de’ikko giyoogaa.
I issi kutti haysedan, Doona odettiya taarikedan, goobatettaadan, siiqo medhdhi xaafuwa taarikedan (romance), tumaappe haakkida ammanodan nabbabees.Yohuwan qassi qoncciyan erettida nabbabiyaagaa hanttaara birshshetta hasheto kanchchiya shoobbiya polotikaanne minttetto( moral) halchchuwan ubbay issi kutti eesuwan shiiqees (Adimaasa1995:95).
Gita adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchatu phikettay, Haadiisa Alamaayu, zammaana kilaasiikkaale Siiqoy Hayqqana Gakkanaashin ( Fiqir Iskke Meqaabir)  yaagiya 1958 M.L koyruwan  attamettidaagaa  xaafanchchaay Afiworqqa kaallees. Hagee erettida adussa medhdhi xaafoy   piudaale Tophphiya qaaxxenna   eqotatubaa pilliqidi boriyaagaa ba garssan oyqqiis. Issi kutti siiqobaanne tumubaa gidiya goshshanchchaa bazzaabbanne  biittaa godee  Sebli giddon digettida siiquwa taarikiya yaagiya adussa medhdhi xaafuwa .  Siiqo koshshaanne guyye attida eqotatu hayqo deexuwa giddon de’iya un”oy goshshanchchay siiqanaadan maataa immiyoogaaninne Sebla la’a doonaa (freedom language) yexxin birshshettees. 
Hara adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchati Afiworqqi dooyido ogiyaa ekkidosona. Lamma Manggistu xaafido  Danttuwa  yaa’aa / Ye gixim gubaa’ee( Synod of Poetry) yaagiyaagee 1955 M.L. attamettiis. Mikaa’eela Kabbadi qassikka,  Amaarattuwan aawaa aawaa ceegay ( the grand old man)  xeetu maxaafatuppe bollaa xaafiis. Gidoppe attin ha xeetanne laatamu maxaafatuppe laatamanne naa’u maxaafatu kanchchee attamettiis. I Roomiyoonne Juulet qassikka Faust( Malvaer 1997:74) meezeyiisinne birshshiis.Belawu Girma koyro adussa medhdhi xaafoy  biittay saluwaara oyqettidaba milatiyaasaa pinnin/ ke adimas ba shaager, beyond the horzon/  yaagiyaagee hara barchcheyiyaabaa yootiyoogaaninne  Toophphiya hiyyeesata qohiyoogaa yootiyoogan  aahuwan nashettida bala qofaappe simo adussa medhdhi xaafo.
Tekile Hawaariyaata Gemmechchu Araya yaagiyo prenchche biitta  gidiya  xomoosiya, Mime Dubonne Foi imettida ‘Araya’ omooddo meran imota na’aa  adussa Adbenchcheriya paattidi yootiya timirttiyaawa adussa medhdhi xaafo.  Perenchche biittaa xomoosiyaara efin biis. He biittan tamaaridi yelaga asadan hanidi ba biitti guyye simmiis.Arayay arggo tekinooloojiyaassinne A yishkkatettawu ciimma bonchchuwa dichchiis. Gidikkonne I lo”o gatee de’iyo Toophiya wozanaaba gidiya  lo”o imotadan odettiya maaraa mankkaanne bana haariyoogaa doseesinne nashshees. 
Ha qommon garxxi ekkidi wottido adussa medhdhi xaafoti ha’i wodiyan zammaana Amaaratto Toophphiya bila xifatiya kilaasiikkaaleta.  Xaafeta kaallidi laattiya yeletay kawotu kawuwa Hayile Sillaaseppe garssa baggaara gidiyaadan wudiis. 
Abee Gubeeniya ( 1933/34-1980) keehin adussa ( 602 sinttaa) xaafuwa xaafancchaynne Lennatu ( Baayessi issi na’ay) Toopphiyan  erettida kawotu kawuwa  Tewodroosabaa yootees.Hara adussa medhdhi xaafoy yelettikke/ Aliwoledim/ I do not want to be  born/ giyaagee  ammano dammatettay hanno gakkanaashin ammano maaraa mankkaa xayssiyoogaanne   goshshanchchata ha’i xayida biittaa dureti huqquniyoogaa maaddi qonccissi bessidi Toophphiya Hayile Sillaase piudaale kawotettaa  eqettiya woykko phalqqiya deretetta adussa medhdhi xaafo.
Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy Toophphiya dargge wotaaddara issippetettaa kawotettaa yuussaabaa yootiya hiraaga qofan erettees. Hagee kolenele Menggisttu kaaletan 1974-1991 gakkanaashin Toophphiyan kawotida huqqunnaa kawota.  Ha huqqunna haaruwa bessiyoogan ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy Orwella nashuwaara laggetiya Toophphebadan  qofettiya adussa medhdhi xaafo. Aliwelledim/yelettikke giyaagaa giddon de’iya isiraa’eeleti issisan shiiqidi de’iya issi haaro biittadan xeelettoosona. Hageekka qassi darggen simmidi giigiis.Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy Hayile sillaase kawotettan digettiis. Dargge ba guutta wodiyawu de’ida Diimookiraase xekkan appe  qanttan ekkiis. Gidoppe attin Darggee issitookka huqqunnaa woykko ciqona de’o oge oottidi maacoogaappe guyyiyan Dargge kawotettaa kaalettiyaageeti   ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy tumu eti medhdhido haaruwa wokkaliyaagaa gidiyoogaa aggiyogaa eesuwaara akeekidosona. Yaatiyo gishshawu A adussa medhdhi xaafoy simmidikka digettiis. Abe Gubeyniyaase hayqoy dargge kawotettay ba haarido deriya hooranssiyo dendduwaara gayttees.Darggee Abe Gubeeniya oosuwa geeman mootiyoogawu denddoy Derasiw 1980 yaagiyo  Belawu Girimi xaafido adussa medhdhi xaafuwan A kawotaa sittan shocido gishshataassa. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy  huqqunnaa kawotettaara eqettiyaanne  maataassi tumaa haasayana  danddayenna xafanchchatu de’uwa paaccees.Girimi Gubeniya kottiya kaallidi  tumaa haasayanawu xaliya xafanchchatu qohuwan gididi garssa huqqunna oosota paaccees.  A eeshshaawati I erido eri baynnanne  annaacettiyo abbee baynna  maataawatuppe simmin leemisettoosona.Qassikka A adussa medhdhi xaafoy  eti maataassi keehin yeemottiyoogaa,eta naagetoy baynna hiillatanne eta amarida danota( crimes) mazggabi oyqqees.
Kunddida Eritera zamachchatinne issippetetta haaruwa (state socialism) qofay boshettidoogee bari huuphen I mootiyoobatuppe issuwa. Girimi xaafido naa’antto adussa medhdhi xaafoy Gidana/ Oromai( Enouph) giyaagee daruwa zooxidi biis.  Gidana/Oromai (Enouph) giyaagee ubbaa be’idanne Afirkkaa polotikaa de’uwa shiranawu danddayiyoogaadan maacida markka ooso.Ha adussa medhdhi xaafuwan xaafanchchay ba de’uwaassi hirggidi maataassi tumubaa haasayees.   Gidana/Oromai/ giyaagee tumukka attamettida Girma saama geetettees. Kawuwa gaazexaa, Addis zemeniya harummiyaagaa gidi simmidi erissuwa( naqaasha) moocona (information minister) xaaxi waaxi kaalettiyaagaa gidida xaafanchchay wurssettan dargge kawotettan penqqeshettidi hara ay oosuwaanne oyqqennaadan digettis.  Girimi Derasiw giyo adussa medhdhi xaafuwawn ba hayquwa hiraagidi taani coo dussaa de’iyoogaappe haraa de’uwa waani de’anaakko  giyoogawu ayba halchchoynne baawa yaagidi xaafiis. Ta de’uwawu halchchoy coo duussaa de’iyoogaa yaagiis. Taani ha adhdho de’uwa, Abiraamedan soon de’ennan qassikka muusedan ta duufoy de’iyoosaa ooninne erennan de’ana yaagiis.
 Taani adhdhidabaa guyye xeelladanne qassikka sinttanawu de’anaaga hidootada  de’ananne xaafana (Girma1980:209).Toophphe ba biittaa utettan shaaettidi de’iyoogaappe denddidaagaaninne  wolqqaa haaruwa mino hanotan teqqiyoogaappe denddidaagan xeetan qoodettiya layttaa hara Afirkkaa biittatuppe duuxxidaba gidikkonne, Toophphiya bila xifatee kumetta Toophphiyaaninne Afirkkan erettidaagaa. Siwahile bila xifatee tumu kumetta Afirkkaa bila xifatedan dicciis. Yohuwan qassi, ha meeziyan kare biittatu sugettay keehin mino. Qassikka wolqqa haaruwaappe denddaagan, Arshsho Afirkkan Swaahillettuwa haasayiya heeratun Inggilizetto bila xifatee keehin xoqqa sohuwa oyqqiis. Hagee Toophphiya bila xifatee gomppaaninne  murutatettan dumma gidanaadaaninne qassikka Toophphiya bila xifatee tumu Afirkkaa bila xifatiya gidiya awugaappenne aadhdhees. A xanna’iyoogee minttettiyaagaanne kare biittatussi deexxiyaaba.Gaasoynne Amaarattoy Gi’iziyaappe keehin deexxiyoogaanne dariya baggi gal”a ogiyan tamaarettiyoogaa. 
Kawotu kawuwa (emperor) Toophphiya kunddettaynne issippetetta (socialist) denddoy Toophphiyaassi ooratta hidootaa ehiis. Dumma dumma qommo pilggettatinne teqettati de’ikkonne  laamiya xuussaappe (1974) simmin naa”u tammu layttatun  (two decades)  kase hani erenna wolqqaama medhdhi xaafo bila xifatiya gogettay Toophphiyan beettiis. Hegawu gaasoy guutta miishshan maxaafati nabbabiyaageetussi aahuwan gishettidosona. Hegaappe simmin Laatamantto xeetu layttaa wurssettan gatee xoqqoogaappenne hara ikkoonoome pacaappe denddaagan bila xifatiya miishshati guuxxi guuxxi biidosona.  Hara Afirkkaa biittatuugaadan, Toophphiya bila xifatee deriya ammanttana kajjeeliyogaaninne lo”o deretettaa moliyoogan go”aa gatee de’iyoobadan ekettees. Gidoppe attin ha higgiyaassi dummayi xeelliyoobati de’oosona. Habteyeesa Yilimi muleera allaxisso halchchuwan pilggetta taarikiya (detective stories) xaafiis. Qassikka Wudinne Maammoy kuukkulssa taariketa ( spy  stories) xaafiisinne birshshiis.  Keehin daro yelaga asay ha maxaafata nabbabidosona.   Amarida Romanttike woykko siiqo taariketi, dariya baggi birshshettan, nabbabiyaageetussi beettidosona.  Hagee malaatiyoogeekka, bila xifatiyan kare biittaagaa laacci xeelliyoogee Toophphiya nabbabo meeziya minttettiyoogaa. 
Amaarattoy loddan Toophphiya timirtte keettatun timirtte imettiyo doonadan haggaazanawu yoogaappe denddaagan, A bila xifatee kumetta Toophphiyan de’iya asaassi ayba metoynne baynnan gakkiyaagaa gidiis. Timirtte keettan imettiya timirtte qommotu ubbaa maxaafaykka Amaarattuwan xaafettiis. Hagee qassi he doonaa caddi oyqqidi xanna’iyoogawu kaalettiyoogaanne cora qaalaa kochchata (dictionary) attamissiyoogawu gattiis. Ha doonaa dichchay qassi Maheteme –Sillaase Woldde Masqqeleduwa milatiyaageeta minttettidi hara aawu alonne (folklore) leemiso haasayata milatiya   bila xifatiya miishshata attamiyoogawu kaalettiis.  Wurssettan, laatamantto xeetu layttaa wurssettan keehin koshshiya hanidabay kawotu kawotettay (emperor) wulli simmin polotikaa dirbbaa (turmoil) gaasuwan kare biittan de’iyoogaa doorida Toophphiya asatuppe puttu giida qeeri bête bila xifatiya. Toophphiya Diyaspporaa ( Diyaspora) bila xifatee bari huuphe de’uwan  keehin dichchiiddi de’ees. 
1.2. Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya Bila Xifatiya
Meeziya-4
Ane kaalliya oyshata waattan gididi tobbidi zaaruwa immite
1.	Toophphiya timirtte mooconatuuninne hara ayso sohotun Briitena kelttiya gelanaadan kaalettidabay aybee?
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2.Inggilizettoy Toophphiya xaafanchchatussi  sintta xeera doona gidennaagawu gaasoy aybakko  yootite?
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________

1.2.1. Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya Bila Xifatiya Doomettaa 
Toophphiya haydaawanne (historical) gaannato (diplomatic) gaytotettaa hara alamiyaara 17 tta xeetu layttaa doomettan oottaasu.   Xaalee Toophphiya woraajji simmin,Briittena betida  kawotu kawuwa  Hayile sillaaseera maadettada  Xaaliya iigganawu Toophphiya yaasu.Hagee Biriittene biittaa asay timirtte mocona milatiya Ayso sohotun kelttiya geliyoogaa kaalettiis.Daro Briittene biittaa asay Toophphiya zammaana timirtte keettatun zoriyaageetanne asttamaareta gididosona. Hara baggaara, Inggilizettuwa  haasayiya biittati,  USA nne Kanaaday Toophphiyaara gaannato gaytotettaa oottidosona. Eti Inggilizetto doonaa tamaarissiyo timirttiyan Toophphiya maaddidosona.  Hegaappe simmin, peranssatto  doonaa bollatettaa sohuwa Inggilizetto doonay ekkiis.  Ingglizettoy Toophphiya timirtte keettatun  timirttee imettiyo doona. Yelaga Toophphiya asay ha doonaara meezetiis. Harinne haraashin Tungga woykko Addisaaba yunbburshshiya tamaareti ha doonaa bila xifate doonadan   wolddayinnuwa woykko danttuwa / poetery/ meezetiyoogaa doommiis. Gidikkonne, Inggilizetto doonay Toophphiya xaafanchchatussi sintta xeeran dooriyo doona gidenna, gidikkabeenna. Gaasoykka eti bila xifatiya oosota Gi’iziyaaninne Amaarattuwan dichchiichchidosona. Toophphiya asay hara Afirkkaa biittatuugaadan  Inggilizetto  doonaa sintta xeera doonadan go’ettokkona. B. Mariyaama Sahile sillasetuwa milatiya amarida xaafanchchati he doonaa  go’ettidi salo sa’a gufantto nabbabiyaageeta gakkanawu Inggilizettuwan xaafiyoogaa doommidosona. Biron doommiyaageeta gidiyoogan lo”o hanotan Afirkkaa Xaafanchchatu mazggabaa giddo gelidosona. 
Hara baggaara qassi kiroosa Teoddiroosi Inggilizettuan Toophphiya bila xifatiya ha kaalliyaagaadan tobbiis.
Afirkkaa kaciya heeratun Inggilizettuwan medhdhi xaafuwa qaxuwaatoy de’ees. Ha lo”o erettida tumaa philqqi guussan Toophphiyan Ingglizettuwan xaafiyo puttu guussay keehin malaaliya ooratta dichcha. Perenssattoy adussa wodiyawu Toophphiya eranchchatussi walaha doona( lingua franca) gidikkonne, 1941 simmin Ingglizettuwaassi sohuwa yeddiis ( Zawuda 1991:108-109). Ha sohoy Xaaliya woraajjuwa, olaa wodiyan, Ingglize biittan sheephetuwa  ekkidi de’iya kawotu kawuwa Hayile Sillaasee simmi makkin darin minniis. Olaappe simmin, Inggilizetto doonay pirdda keettatuuninne kawo ooso keettatun erettidi Toophphiya timirtte keettatuununne yunbburshshetun timirtte doona gidiis. 
Hara guutta Inggilizetto xaafoy hara wogatussi (cultures) oorattatettan yeemottiyoogaappe denddidaagaaninne olaappe simo wodee denttettiyaagaa gididoogan 1960aappe kasiyan dommiis. Kare biittan de’iyaanne Diyasppora xaafanchchata gidida amarida Toophphiya xaafanchchati Inggilizettuwa naa”antto doonadan ekkidosona.  Haraati Inggilizettuwaaninne doona dooyido doonatun  xaafidosona. Ha xaafanchchati Awurooppaa bila xifatiya molettata banttabaadan ootti ekkidi I maayettiyo meratu woykko qottatu xallan xaafana danddayoosona. Inggilizetto doonay Toophphiya xaafanchchatun doorettido gaasoti xaafanchchatuppe xaafanchchatun dummatoosona.Issooti issooti coo be’ana, puulaa dooriyo hanotan haraatussi qassi ha aahuwan salo sa’a gufanttuwan goggiya doonan aaho deriyaakko gakkanawu  ogiya demmanawu injjetiyoogaa. Gidoppe attin, Inggilizettuwan xaafiyaaba gidikkonne, ha ubba xaafanchchatikka bantta sheniyan bantta Toophphiya / Afirkkaa  baaso denddo oottida tumaa gelissidi Toophphiya de’o hanotaabaa xaafoosona.  
B.M. Sahile Sillaase IngglizettuwanToophphiya xaafuwan bollati beettiis. A oyddantto  Ingglizetto medhdhi xaafoy  Eexxiya Mittata/ Fire Brands/  yaagiyoogee A oosuwa keehin lo”o oosodan xeelissiis. Gaasoykka polotikanchchatuura eqettanawu assi de’iya yaa haa geligenchchenna equwa.  Abara Taaddasi ha oosuwa Puulanchchati Hanno Gakkanaashin Yelettibookkona/The Beautiful Ones Are Not Yet Born/(Aderanne Ahimeda 1995b:164)  yaagiyo Ayi Kwei Armaahsa oosuwaara annaaciis. Hara qassi keehin abbiyaara de’iyaanne darin erettibeenna xaafanchchati adussa medhdhi xaafotanne tiyaatire kaassata Inggilizettuwan xaafidosona. Gubeniya Abee, Amaaratto doonan xaafido laatamu maxaafatuppe gujuwa, naa”u maxaafata Ingglizettuwan xaafiis (Molvaer 1997:183). US giddon de’iya Iow Yunbburshshiyan mero xaafuwa( creative writing) xanna’ida  Worqqu Dayinnaachchoy  1973n attamettida Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa( The Thirteenth Sun) yaagiyo adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafiis. Gebire Mediina Tsaagaayee tiyaatire kaassatanne  danttota  Inggilizettuwaaninne Amaarattuwan xaafiis( Molvaer 1997:272). Ha gita danttanchchaanne woykko wolddayinnuwaanne(poet)  Diraamaatisttiya  oosoy Biodun Jefiyon ha guussan lo”o kuuyettiis.  “ kawotu kawuwa (emperor) xuusaappe kase Toophphiya (pre-revolutionary) A ayyaanaama ammano ayissobatanne A haaruwaabay ubbay deretetta awudiyan (context) odettees.Afirkkaa Kambriijje( Cambridje) Taarikenne deays de’ays giya deriya ixxiya Karibiya( carbean) bila xifatiya, Gebire Mediina tiyaatire kaassati keehin mino, heennaa denttettiya annaaciyan kumida ammanota oyqqees, hagee qassi qofaa minttettiyoogaa, wolqqa bessiya kawotettay kawotennaadan oottiyoogaanne haaruwa( state) guuttiyoogaa”(Jefiyo,1995:186)
Gujuwan Tewodiroosa Bogaalee (2008) InggilizettuwanToophphiya bila xifatiya doomettaabaa qonccissees. Attamoy (publication) Toophphiya bila xifatee Inggilizettuwan doommanaadan gaaso gididabatuppe issuwa.Zammaana aaho deriya timirttee MinilikeII timirtte keettaa keexuwaara 1990 M.L Toophphiyan doommiis qassikka he wodiyan daro  wuday kare doonaa tamaarissiyoogawu imettiis( Tekesta,1996). Daro asttamaareti  Gibxeppe (Egypt) yiida bila eran ka’idaageeta. Daro kare biittaa asttamaareta hasheyidoogee, kare biittaa doonata timirtte doona oottanawu sintta xeera gaaso. Hagaappe denddaagan timirtte polisiyan doona timirtte qommoti bollati beettidosona. Tekestte (Ibid S 10) ha xinaatiyan giiddi  “ ba de’iyo koyro laatamantto laytta wodiyan Minilik II timirtte keettay timirtte keettadan gidennan doonaa eqotadan (language institude) xeelettees. Perenssatoy, Xaalettoynne Arebettoy, Amaarattuwa kaallidi bayra timirtte qommota.
Hayle sillaase I kawotettaa wodiyan, ciimma tamaarisso wogay merettiis. Qassikka daro Toophphiya asay xoqqa timirttiyawu kare biitti biidosona. I xaalee Toophphiya oyqqi simmin 1941 Briittene yarati/staff/  Toophphiya yiidosona qassikka loddaara  Briittena Toophphiyan  kelttetiyaaro gidaasu.Hegaappe denddaagan,“Tungga( Adisaaba) timirtte keettata aawatettan kaalettiyaageetinne timirtte mooconan waanna zoriyaageeti Britene asata.”(Girma,1964 M.L,338). Hegaappe denddaagan, timirttee imettiyoy Inggilizettuwaana. Hegaappe guyyiyan Inggilizettoy Toophphiyan kawo kare (foreign) doonadan ekettiis.( Ibid:337).Tamaarisso polo buussaa minttettanawu, tamaarissuwawu darin haniya miishshati Briiteneppe yaanaadan oosettiis.Naa”antto xekkaa timirtte keettaa yeddiyo paacetikka Briitenne yunbburshshiyan giigidosona.
Hagaappe hara nu biittiya hara biittatuura lo”o gaytotettaa aassishin Toophphiya yiida timirttiya miisoonetuppe (educational missioneries) daroti Inggilizettuwa haasayiya Kanaadanne (Canada) USA milatiya biittata. Ha gaasuwan, he wodiyan, kare biittaa doonaa tololayoy, harinne haraashin Inggilizettuwaagee  keehin gujjiis. Gaasoykka daro wuday ha kare doonaa tamaarissuwawu imettiis. “ Ha biittaa deretettaa misiliya laammanawu doommida zammaanatetta polo buussay kare biitta doonan luxida tamaareta gidiyaadan eesuwan loohissiyoogaa kaalettiis(Ibid,1996:103).
Ha biittee taarikiyan zammaana timirttiyawu banqqatida woykko hanida  bayrabatuppe  issoy 1950 M.layttan merettida  Tungga/ Adisaaba / yunbburshshiya kolloojjiya. Ha yunbburshshee dooyettin keehin cora laameti yiidosona.Yelaga Toophphiya asay bantta biittan xoqqa timirttiya qaadaa demmidosona. Ha yunbburshshiyan erettida tamaarissiyaageeti kare biitta asata.Qassikka timirttee aadhdhiyoogeekka Ingglizettuwaana. Hegaa gishshatawu killoojjeekkaToophphiya Ingglizetto danttuwa,wolddayinnuwa (poetry) yuussawu hara ooso.
Ane Toophphiya asan xaafettida Inggilizetto bila xifatiya be’oos. Ha bila xifatiya oosoti danttuwa/ wolddaanuwa/ (poetry) qantta taarikiya, adussa medhdhi xaafuwaanne diraamaa qommotussi shaakettana danddayoosona. Ane koyrottidi danttuwan/wolddayinnuwan / tobettaa doommoos.
1.2.2.Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya  Bila Xifatiya Qommota 
Meeziya -5
Ane kaalliya oyshata waattan gididi tobbidi zaarite
1.Amaaratto bila xifatiyaappenne Inggilizetto bila  xifatiyaappe kasetidi Toophphiyan doommidaagee awugee?
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2. Toophphiya xaafanchchatun xaafettida Inggilizetto mero xuufeti oyqqiyoobati :aybee aybee?
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________ 
1.2.2.1. Danttuwaanne danttanchchaa (Poetry and poets)  
Toophphiya xaafanchchatun xaafettida Inggilizetto mero xuufeti oyqqiyoobati :-Medhdhi xaafuwa, diraamaanne danttuwa woykko wolddayinnuwa.Gidoppe attin, bila xifatiya xaafettay Inggilizettuwan qaxuwaati ekkees. Nuuni Toophphiyan xaafettida bila xifaiya qoppiyoode, Inggilizettuwaaraanne Amaarattuwaara geeddariyoodiyan I keehin dalggi beettiyoy Amaarattuwaana gidiyoogaa demmoos. Amaaratto bila xifatee daro wodiyawu  meezeti simmiina Inggilizetto bila xifatee yiidoy.Ha biittee bila xifatiya qaaxota pilggiya Beer(1975) milatiya amarida pilgiyaageetiToophphiya bila xifatee Ingglizettuwan aadhdhida tammu layttatu ayfe giidi palamoosona. Qassikka Huntsbeger ( 1970), ba “Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya bila xifatiya anttirooppooloojiya”yaagiyo xuufiyan giiddi hagaa mala  bila xifatee ussuppun tammaawa dichchaa yaagiis.
Nuuni Toophphiya danttuwa woykko wolddayinnuwa kase pulttuwa Inggilizettuwan qoppiyoode, naa”u ano yohota demmoos.Hegeetikka “ Toophphiya Heralddiyaanne” “ Tungga woykko Addisaaba yunbburshshiya kolloojjiya” gaazeexaa attamuwa harinne haraashin he yunbburshshiya tamaareti bila xifatiya wogaa woykko meeziya minttettanawu baaso gaasodan xeelettoosona. Toophphiya Heraldde gaazeexaa attamoy qassi Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya danttuwa woykko wolddayinnuwa (poetry) doomettawu wolqqaa immiis.Leemisuwawu “Toophphiya Heralddee” (Gom-1pd.45, Laabboshsha 6, 1944M.l.,St 3)attamettiyo koyro heeran Toophphiya danttuwa woykko wolddayinnuwa attamettiyo koyro heeran Toophphiya danttanchchaa woykko wolddayinnuuwaa(poet) , Inggida Tsigge Hannan xaafettidoogaadan  issi Inggilizetto danttoy de’ees. Ha danttuwawu huuphe yohoy “ Xoonettenna la’atettaa”/”Un conquered Soverign”/. Hagee Toophphiya danttanchchan (poet) xaafettida koyro Inggilizetto danttodan xeelettees.Toophphiya Heraldde 1943 merettiis. 
 Toophphiya herald (Heralddee) kase attamotun “ Danttanchchaa gaxaa”/ The poets  Corner /yaagiya huupe yohuwa amdee( column) de’ees. Hagee qassi ubbatoo danttuwaakko woykko wolddayinnuwaakko baqqees.  Kare biittaa asatu imotay (contribution) ha gaazeexan Toophphiya  danttanchchati danttuwa xaafanawu wolqqaa immidoogaadan qofettees. Toophphiyan xaafettida naa”antto danttoy 1961 M.L. attamettiis.  He danttoy “ Baletettidaagaa”(“Deluded”) geetetti xeesettiya bayyana Alulan (Toophphiya Heralddiya,Caljjo12,1961 M.l sint.2) xaafettidaagaa. Tumukka ha danttuwaappe kase 1956 M.L erettenna  danttanchchan xaafettida hara danttoy de’ees. Xaafanchchay erettenna gishshatawu kare asatu danttokko  woykko Toopheba gaanawukko meto.  Danttoy “ issi guuttabaa xalla,” ( Toophphiya Heraldde, Bullaala 24,195, sintt.2).
1944 M.L. biidi 1961 M.L garssan yunbburshshiya tamaareti bantta attamotun, daro danttota  attamidosona.Yunbburshshee merettiyo kase gallassatu wodiyan yunbburshshiya kamppaasiya giddon dumma tamaaretu qaattati polettidosona.Tamaaretu goshshanchchatunne kataman de’iya cora asaa moorettida hanotaa eridoogee qaaxuwa shoobbanawu xeellin  beettiya baaso gidiis (Bahira 1995). Yohuwan qassi, hagaa ubbaappe kasiyan, “ kase layttatu tamaareti la’a gaazeexaa attamuwaanne la’a maabaraa( free press and free  union ) baaxiyan erettoosona(Ibid,222). Ha qaattay naa”uban ayfiis.-yunbburshshiya tamaaretu issippetettaa woykko mabaraa 1959nne yunbburshshiya tamaaretu gaazeexaa/ metseetiya, oduwaanne hayyuwa” (1959 M.L) nne  “baaxiya”(1967 M.L). Ha gaazeexan woykko metseetiyan polotikaanne hara issippetetta allaalleti he wode tamaaretun xaafettidaageeti beettidosona.Tamaariya xaafanchchati dumma dumma bila xifatiya qottata  bantta qofaa qonccissanawu go’ettidosona. Hegeetuppe issoy wolddayinnuwa/danttuwa/ (poetry). Ha gaazeexati woykko metseeteti aadhdhido doonay Inggilizettuwa.Ha doonaa aarettan doommida mino meezee Toophphiya Inggilizetto danttoy woykko wolddayinnoy mokki ayifanawu lo”o meeze. 
“Odotunne Hayyotu” kase attamotuppe Inggilizetto Toophphiya danttuwan woykko    wolddayinnuwan koyrodan xeelettiya amarida danttota demmoos. Hagee qassi Toophphiya    heralddiyan koyro attamettida danttotakka haphphi oyqqees.   Dumma dumma kase attamotu woshettay bessiyoogaadan, “Odotinne ayfe  hayyoti” dumma dumma Toophphiya danttota Inggilizettuwan attamanawu sintta xeeran beettiyaageeta. Ha attamuwan beettida koyro danttoy, Baalu Girma (News and Views) / Odotanne Hayyota, gomp.III pd.5 sintta.3 Baraata ,13,1959 M.L)  xaafettida “Qaareta” (“Apes”) giyaagaa. Qassikka Baalewu Girman(Ibid) xaafettida “ kallachchata” (“Crowns) giyaagaanne Gabayo Mekibeben xaafettida( Ibid.pd.6, sintta 4, Baraata 20,1959 M.L) “ Taani shemppuwa gishshatawu yeekkana”(I cry for  a soul) yaagiyaagaa.  Kaalliya danttoti 1960tun attamettidosona.  Kase tamaaretu danttanchchatuppe   Toophphiya  bila xifatiya taarkiyan laamiya ehaana baaxetidaageeta demmoos. Hegeetuppe koyro xeesettiyaagee kumetta Toophphiya kantti kiyiyi nabbabettiya adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchaa Girma Baala.  I kase danttanchchatuppe daro danttota xaafidoogan erettidaagaa. A danttoti “Qaareta” (“Apes”), “Kallachchata”(“Crowns”) nne “Pootuwa Pireemiya”( “Photo Frame”) “ Mal”aa Cammaa geenna Pulttuwa (“Fountains of Non sense”) , Qamma Hanotaa(“Noctural Mood”) “ Sarotaa”( “Greetings”) nne “ he haahosan de’iya zanggaarata (Those Yonder Hiills”). A danttotuppe dariya baggati dumma dumma asaa de’o hanotatubaa yootoosona.
Yunbburshshiya tamaaretu bila xifatiya imotay “Odotanne” “Ayfe Hayyota” giyaageetu xallan zeerettenna. I oyqqiyo heeray aakkidi  1962 M.L. daro baggi bila xifatiya oosotu xallan baxuuxiya hara magiziinee( gaazeexay) beettiyoogaa doommiis. Ha magaziiniya woykko gaazeexaa huuphe yohoy “1962 M.L biidi 1967 M.L. gakkanaashin attamettida” issibaa.yaagiyaagaa. Ha yunbburshshiya tamaaretu bila xifatiya magaziiniyan dumma dumma bila xifatiya oosota,dumma dumma huuphe yohootuuninne timirtte qommotun qantta taarikiya, danttotinne darissoti beettidosona.I attamettiyo wodiyan ha magaziiniyan, laatamu danttotuppe bollay Inggilizettuwan attamettidosona. Ha magaziniyan koyro danttoy Ariaya Iyaasuugaa,” issibaa naagiyoogaa”(Issibaa,gomp.II pd1, sint.28 1962 M.L )Ha magaziniyawu hara danttoti “ Duriyaanne Hiyyeesaa”(“ The Rich and The Poor) Taaddasa Takilen xaafettidaagaanne Coolle Ishatun xaafettida ‘ retrospect( zaari hassayuwa),Xumaa (Darkness), Kajjeeluwa(“Trial”), Xiskkuwa” (Sleep) nne” wodiya”(Time) geetettiyaageeta. 1967 M.L hachchi gakkanaashin attametti kiyidabatun Inggilizettuwan bila xifatiya magaziinee ha biitten attamettibeenna.   
Dichchatuppe amaridaageeti bessiyoogaadan bantta attamota wolqqaa immidoogaadan qofettees. Gidikkonne hagaappe haray denddanawu bessiya issi baaso yohoy de’ees.  Layttan layttan tamaaretu giddon xifatiya  annaacee polettanaadan oosettiis. Green Field (1969) qonccissiyoogaadan, 1961 aappe doommidi danttuwa/wolddayinnuwa/ annaacee yunbburshshiya taamaaretu garssan de’iis.  Annaaciya giddoppe keehin lo’o danttoti nabbabettidosona. Ha wogay siree baynnan “ Odotuuninne”  “ Ayfe markkata” “Issibaa,” nne hara attamotun naqaashettida bila xifatiya meezeta denttettidosona. Kaalliya danttoti kase wodetun xaafettida danttotuppe amaridaageeta.
QAARETA
“ Ne duriyo durssaa  ta dosayiis 
Ne qaaxxiyo qaaxuwa,
I  issuwa ekkees yohuwan qassi  ayfe liphodan
Ta neessi hegaadan yootanawu  aynne sirikke”
Cuway   carkkuwa bollan  tuqituqidi cuwattees
Ubbaa  oyqqiya  keettay ariisinne woddiis  
Eti yaanne    haa  wuxakettoosona
Muzunqqay  toli oyqqidi sinttawu biis
“ neeni   qommo saaloppe yiida 	
Kiitanchcha
Ha  murunetti qashetti uttida  shaaraa mentta
Ha murunno siiquwa.”
I  ayfee A ayfiyaara gayttiyoode  ba menttershshaa qalam’’ada qaattawusu,
Tama bonqquwaadan zo’ida  I doonay  malaalees,
Qaalatu kanchchee barchcheta poliis
Ayyiyaana qaariyawu !Hara qaaree xoonees!
                                             Girma  Be’ala ( 1959)
OGIYAAWAA ( TRAVELER)
Taani irxxanne  barjjiya qamma
Taani dum’’a maataa bollan zokkuwan bonggottada  zin”idoogaadan 
Qofay  ta  kahaa kanttidi kiyees.
Gidduwaan  saluwa xoolinttetu  eettay de’ees 
Taassi  kisaaray siyettiis.
 Imatta biittan ogiyaawaa  kisaaraa
Hassayenna yashshay ta wozanaara dozhgu gi  kantti kiyiis,
Yohotu  qofay  keehin aduqqidi bees qassikka yohoti  yaanawu
 Qassikkata daafura bollay kokkoriisinne kinchchuwan donjjilliis.
Alamee asa biitta gidennaagaa  eriyo gishshawu,
Imatta, boshettibeenna, nne ubbatoo yelaga.
Taani ta biyo  haahuwa  issi kutti  qoppaas
Qassikka yaana de’iya haahuwa,
Qassikka daafurida ogiyaawaa  hedhdhettaa
Ta ha alamee sinttawu baanaadan  oottana
“Taani  keehi imatta biittaa giddon de’iya  ogiyaawaa”
Kaalettiyaabi baynna ogiyaawaa,
Aadhdhiyoossi baynna biittaa.
Coolle  Ishshata,1962
Hayqoy ba araataa  anhaa umbban  essiis.
Hagan kayyoy ufayissaa, wooqay de’o
Xeetantta layttata kanttidi yiida  benibaa,
Co’atettay karettatettay poo’o gidiyoosaa diggees
Xottiyan xottiyan xottidi,
Suuttaynne  seerida asaa ashoy 
Suuttaynne  seerida asaa ashoy
Kuwaa giddon musiis,guliyaadan xa’yidi-
Issi kotteenne  attibeenna,wodee baynna bidintta xallay
Hayqqoy ha haaruwan  wozanappe  miiccees,
Xeella xiniqa, guutta asata, qariqanttiyaadan zuummiyaageeta
Hagaabiya ta shemppo ambbaa,nne doga
Neeni  ha   barchcheyiyaa ne alamiya gidadasa
Hagoosa Tekola (1962) 
Toophphiya danttoy Inggilezettuwan beettiyogawu hara gaasoy Toophphiya  xaafanchchati Luma Gezo nabbabiyaageeta gakkanawu de’iya eta buzo koshshaa/Yeemuwa.  Toophphiyan  erettida Inggilizettuwa adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchatuppe B.Maariyaama artikiliya( pilggetta xuufiya ), “Baatta Giddo Xomppiya”/ “Yegan Meberat” giyoogee Toophphiya bila xifatee kare biittaa nabbabiyaageetuuninne borinashshiyaageetun ixettanaadan oottida haasayaanne shoobiyaa. Hagawu gaasoy,ha artikiliya xaafanchchay giidoogaadan, tumatettan nu bila xifatee hara alamee erenna doonantun  xaafettidoogaa. (Toophpiya Heralddiya Gool .20, 1974 M.L.) Inggilizettuwaaninne hara kare biitta doonatun xaafida amarida Toophphiya xaafanchchati kare biitta nabbabiyaageetun nabbabettiyo qaadaa  demmidosona.G/Mediina Tsaggaayeenne  Darasa Solomoni bantta danttonne/ Wolddayinonne hara oosotun xeesettana dandayoosona . Amaarattuwaappe gujuwan , Tsagaaye daro danttota Inggilizettuwan xaafiis. Solomona Darasi, hara baggaara, naa”u  aahuwan  erettida doonatun, Inggilizettuwaaninne  Frenssattuwan, xaafiis.  I amaarattuwankka xaafees qassikka anttota shiishshiyoogan erettees.
Nuuni danttuwaabaa/ wolddayinnuwaa qoppiyoode, dumma dumma magazeenetuununne gaazeexatun attamettida daro danttota demmoos. Toophphiya danttuwa/wolddayinnuwa Inggilizettuwan attamida attamotuppe  “Odotunne”  “Ayfe hayyotu”/ “ News” and “ Views”,/ “Issibaa”/ “Something”, “Toophphiya Heralddiya,”/ The Ethiopian herald/,“ToophphiyaXeelliyaagaa,”/“Ethiopian Obsrver”/, "Toophphiya Zaari xeeluwa,” “ Ethiopian Reviewer,”Longgiya”/ “Yekatit,/” “Afirkkaa Bila erata,”/ Afirkan Arts,” “ Gaytettaanne Kifile Gadaawaa”/ “Link and Monitor,” geetettiyaageeti sintta xeeran  de’iyaageeta. Qassikka Toophphiya xaafanchchatun  attamettida amarida Inggilizetto Danttuwa/ wolddayinnuwa  maxaafati de’oosona. Hegeetikka –G.E.Gorfu,Wildoats (1974 M. L),  Qofaa, nne barkatettaa Danttota (1974 M. l.),/ poems of  thought and Solitude (1974 E. C),Asesefa G. M.T  Cengurssaa /The voice( 1980 M.L), Hama Tuma, of  spades Ethiopians( 1991), Lemleme Tsegaw siyettibeenna cenggurssata /un heard voices/( 1994) nne  Aayee ayfe hayyuwa/ A mother’s Eye View/( 1997) ,Biruk Kebede,The Son Themba (2001) and Afirkka Distracted by  Daniel Legese (2001). Amarida  hara danttoti Karetta Afirkka danttota /Poems of Black Afirka (1975) milatiya dumma dumma lo”o danttuwa/ wolddayinnuwa  nibaabetu( Anthologies of poetry) giddon attamettidosona .Hagaappe gujuwan Tsegaye danttoti Apiro –Eezhiya  danttuwan/ wolddayinnuwa( 1971) nne Afirkka assershiniya /Afirkan  assertion ( 1976)  attamettidosona. Adanttotuppe daroti qassikka  heera magaaziiniyan,  Toophphiya Xeelliyaagaa/ Ethiopia Observer nne perenssaatto  attamoti a French  Publication,  ha’i de’iya Afirkkaa/  Presence Afirka/ giyaageetun beettidosona  Deresa Solomonikka ba danttota Amerikkaa  Bila Eraa Metseetiyan, Afirkaa Bila Eraa ( America Art Journals), Afirkan Arts 
Ta Kushiya Oyqqa (Hold My Hand)
Oyqqa ta kushiya karetta aayee, oyqqa,
Taani diccana koyyayiis,Taani ta tohotun eqqana koyyayiis
Diccanaassi, eqqanaassi, nne mootanaassi.
Taani ne karetta xanttaa xammanawu digettidaba gidikkonne
 Yelaga mal”iya kafotu qefeti xubettiyaaba/ bollaa qohoy de’iyoogeeta  gididaba gidikkonne 
Ne micettida qesetuppe  Taani  sheniya kessanawu koyyayiis
De’uwa kessanawu,minotettaa kessanawu
Ne micettida qesetu suutta xaphotu giddon goggiyaagaappe hidootaa kessanawu.
Karetta aayee taani   ne qanttaappe xayida na’aa
 Worddo siiquwan boshettida/ abortive/ shiiliya/ suuttazeero
Ciimma xumaa garssan wontta gidiis 
Taani taarikiya hayqo-ayfiya giddon de’iya gilqqida  guutta na’aa
Erettenna ha’i ta sunttay 
Gidikkonne issitookka  taani tumu sunttaa ekkoogaappe Karettaa Aayee
Chaakka wolqqaama ayyaanaa sunttaa malaa 	
Numaaquwa,Hereero ayyaanaa sunttaa malaa 
Zululanddeegaa, Matabeleegaa…
Hegaappe guyyiyan taani boshettida ne haatta qanttaa/ womb/   shiiliya  gidikke 
 Hegaappe guyyiyan  taani keehin mino ne zerettata gidiya   attuma naatuppe issuwa 
Taani ne  daro layttaa  qoodissida ammano wogatu bonchchuwaassi keettaattenne
Taani ne olatu, ne zerettatu durssatu bonchchuwaassi  keettaattenne
Ne shaareechchotu gadaawattenne 
Neeni ayyiyo ne la’a miichchaa bonchcho keettaattenne
…….suntti tawu de’idoy zino xalla, tumu sunttay .
Yeellaa.  Hara bonchchoy ha’i baawa ……Karetta aayee  neenaara  dapparettiis/ rapped/
Hara miichchi baawa yohuwan qassi A qilliico cabbuwaappe……
La’a miichchay ta garssan anha 
Ixettidaagaa xallay xoonuwa…Waaanada taani IXXIKKINAA 
Wurssetta siiqoy tanan attibeenneeyee
Nena dapparidaageetu xugunttaa giddon ta de’anaadan tana maaddanawu
Ta Karetta Aayee imattaa  ta neekko ehoo
La’a miichchaa bonchcho sohuwan  ixettidaageetu siiquwa…
Yohuwan qassi  issi uri ay naagii 
Balan pude  xoqqissiyo  worddo siiqoy worddo  xaphuwaara….
Hachchi  omarssa xallan  taani aymuwa  aymottaasi Karetta Aayee 
Hagee akeekanawu aymottiyo aymoo 
Ne    zerettatu  bayra henttanchchati ubbay kushshiya issippe gattiyoogaa  aymottaasi
Ta mala bayratikka  kushshiya issippe gattidosona, som’’uwa som’’uwaarakka gattidosona
Wozanaakka gattidosona……..oyshaa denttanawu …..
…  “ Nu giddoppe xayiday oonee…oonee.”
Oyqqa ta kushiya Karetta Aayee, oyqqa,
Taani zaaruwa immanawu diccana koyyayiis.
Taani ta mala bayratussi ta tumu sunttaa immana koyyayiis.
Taani ta uddufun tammanne uddufun ishantti koyyiiddi de’iyo xayida dorssa
Oyqqa ta kushiya,taani  ta tohotun eqqana koyyayiis, taani  diccana koyyayiis.
Taani Alamiya mootana koyyayiis,Karetta Aayee, oyqqa.
Gebre Mediina Tsaggaaya, 1965 
1991 M.L.doommidi wotaaddara kawotettay kunddi simmin,ooratta danttuwa xaafanchchati (poets) Toophphiya bila xifatiya oosuwan dumma dumma lo”o nibaabe xuufetuura beettidosona. Leemisuwaassi, Kabbada Buruka Tumbbu na”aa/ The Son of Thumbu/(2001) nne Ta Maatafaa/  My Seal/ (2003),Yemaana Fikire selaama The poetaster (1999-book one part one), Hayle Alema Vent to Stifled Emotions(2003),nne Fondant( Peony and Fiction), 2a, 1( 2006), Kabbada  Luulitinne  Mulaatu Wosene The rebbon of Heart(2004), Meti Shewaye  Yilima The Gate way(2005), Kidaane Yemaana(Jamaica) Soaring Sprits, Menbere Ruuta The Blessed Ocean on the Land of Sin( 2007), Alemu Asaffa Manacled(2012)  yaagettiyaageeti Coratuppe  amaridaageeta . 

Yeletay Inggilizettuwan xaafanaadan minttettiyoogee woykko salo sa’a gufantto  nabbabiyaageta gakkanawu koyyiyoogee minotettaadan xeelettees, oyshaykka murutaa/ quality/. Nuuni qommota, dichchaa pilliqi oychchiyoode , nuuni  Darasa Solomanne G/Mediina  milatiya danttotun  qommuwa geelladan demmennan  aggana danddayoos. G/ Mediini  generiya biron  doommiyaageetuppe  gididanne  simmidi generiya dichchidaagaa. Tumukka hummunnatettay woykko murutatettay(quality)  coratettaa kaallidi yiyoogaadan ammanetettees. Generiyan  xeelettida ooratta hanotay macca xaafanchchatu hashetuwa. Ane  macca xaafanchchti xaafido danttota be’oos.

Ha  qommogeeti  danttuwaassi huuphe yohota gidishin ane   kaalliya kumetta   danttotakka be’oos.

Yohoti Aadhdhi Wodhdhidosona (Thimgs Fall Apart)
