Hara Toophphiya  Inggilizetto bila xifatiyan  bila xifatiya qommoy adussa medhdhi xaafuwa 
Amarida wodiyaappe simmin wolddayinnuwa (danttuwa) doomettaappe kasiyan, yeda nibaabiya ( prose) bila xifatiya oosoti attamettidosona.
1.2.2.2.  Adussa Medhdhi xaafuwaanne  A xaafanchchata  
Meeziya -6
 Kaalliya  oyshata citan gididi zaarite
1.Ane  intte eriyo Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafotuppe  heezata xaafite.
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2. He qommo adussa medhidhi xaafuwa  xaafanchchati  xaafido adussa medhdhi xaafuwa huuphe yohotuppe na”ata xaafite
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
Adussa medhdhi xaafuwa qommuwa shaakettan, daro oosoti de’oosona.  Hegeetuppe  daroti xaafettidoy he yeleta xaafanchchatun 1960aa waaninne 1970 aawan qassikka simmiyoodiyan hara Toophphiya asatun   xaafettidosona. He wodiyan  attamettida  kase adussa medhdhi xaafuwa oosotuppe Kabbada Ashanaafa,Paaxettaa /Confession/(ca. 1962), Sahile Silaase Birhaane Maariyaama Heezzu  adussa medhdhi xaafota:Afersaata/Afersata/(1969),Olanchcha Kawuwa /Warrior Kings/(1974), Tama mittaa/Fire brands/(1979),Wolde Hayhile, Sunttaa Naaga /Defend The Name/ (ca.1969), Abbe Gubegna yuuqiyuuqennaagaa/  Defiance (1975), nne Dayinnaachewu Worqqu Tammanne Heezzanttaa Awaa/ The Thirteenth Sun ( 1973).  Ha hanotan hagaa  xeelliyaagan  1990 aawan Luule wodiyaappe simmin doommidi xeeraa gakkidoogaadan qofettees. Toophphiya asati,dariya baggi,  Diaspporati,   daro adussa medhdhi xaafuwa oosota  ayfissidosona. 
Melaakkine ( 2005)  bessiyoogaadan issi na”aa gidiya  Amaaraatto oosuwan keehin erettida  xaafanchchatikka Inggilizetto   Adussa medhdhi xaafota, kassata, nne  danttuwa attamidosona. Hegeekka geelladan eranchchatetta meezetiyoogaa ( intellectual exercise)  woykko banttabaa nabbabiyaageeta ( audiences)  corayanawunne  woykko Amaarattuwa  A doddidaageetuppe  la’a kessanaassa gidana danddayees.  Hara baggaara Zeruhun  Asfawu  ba  Yelaga Baaxiya/ The Young Crusades,/ Dabbidaabbiyaanne Kessa Ekka / The Letters and Escape / yaagiyo  adussa medhdhi xaafotu kaseyuwan (preference) qonccissiiddi   bantta kushiya Inggilizetto  medhdhi xaafuwa oosotun meezeyida leemisuwaassi Sahile sillaase Berihaane Maariyaamanne Dagachewu Worqquduwa milatiya  koyro kochchooro xaafanchchati de’oosona. Ha yayinettida  Toophphiya  xaafanchchati Afirkkan layttan layttan  kaallidi attamettiyaagaa giddon  eta oosoy attamettanaadan qaada demmidosona. Sahile sillaase Afersata, Olanchcha Kawuwa / Warrior King/ nne  Tama Mittata/ Fire Brands,/ Daniachu Worqu Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa/ The Thirteenth Sun / geetettiyaageeti bantta wodiyan nabbabettidosona. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoti  dariya baggi  wogatun,/cultures/ nne  xaafanchchati be’ido  haydaanne polotikaa allaalletun wudees.
Xaaxi waaxuwan, daro eranchchati (scholars)  qommon xeesettida xaafanchchati Afirkkan kaalli kaalli attamissiyo attamo oosuwa  giddon de’iya  xaafanchchatu garssan etikka de’iyoogaadan ammanoosona. Eta adussa medhdhi xaafotu kuuyettatuppe amaridaageeti garssan garxxetti ekettidosona.


Sahilesillaase Berhaane Maariyaama Oosota
Aferssaataa/ afersata/ (1969)
Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy keettaa taman oyttido gaasuwan xuugettida heeran de’iya (villages) Namaaga keettan doommees. Danuwaaway woykko wonjjaliyaaway oonakko pilggi demmanawu, Namaagi Aferssaataa oychchees. Aferssaatay (Amaaratto qaalay) meeze woga meran( traditiona form)  issibaassi  tumaa  demmanawu  halchchida pirddaa hiillaa. Heeran de’iya ubba attumaageetikka hashetanaadan koyettoosona, eta issippetetta xekkay, awugaanne gidikko  I danuwaakkonne  oyshettees, I danuway oonakko erikkokka, woykko danuwaara oyqettidaagan assi ay erinne de’ikkokka. I goyyidi aqiya goshshanchchaasi   keehin gita haro/aqo/ gidiya, ba naatu shemppuwa bollan yaa haa geennan caaquwa caaqqana bessees. Gidoppe attin ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy Tohossa Toophphiyan  Guraage deretun Ciishanna gooshshanchchatu  ha’i  hanotabawu   sitta guyye phoolosso.  Koyruwan Inggilizettuwan xaafettidi,  ha adussa  medhdhi xaafoy wogaa meezeta qonccissiyoogan daro wodiya  wurssiis, qassikka salo sa,a nabbabiyaageetussinne  xaaxi waaxin goyyidi aqiya  gandda goshshanchcha moottatu hanotaa darin erenna   Toophphiya wogga ambba, Tungga( Addisaaba) umbban, de’iyaanne  harinne haraashin qoodan guuxxiya  goshshanchcha moottata.
Olanchcha Kawuwa /The Warior Kings/ ( 1974)
Hagee haydaawa woykko taarikiyaawa adussa medhdhi xaafo, higgeppe kareera yohuwan qassi wurssettan kumetta Toophphiya oyqqi haaridanne barina Toophphiya kawotu kawuwa (Emperor) Kaasa Hayilu yaagi sunttida Kaasa Hayilu  dendduwa taarikiyaabaa yootees. Qoncce annaacissoy taassi Thomas Mofolon xaafettida eranchchanne bila kawuwa Chaakkaara (Chaka),hageekka qassi  Afirkkaa kawotu kawuwa dendduwaabaa  yootiya  haydaawa woykko taarikiyaawa adussa medhdhi xaafo.  Mofoloy  asay maataakko  wolqqan/olan yiyoo issi bussakkiyoobaanne  xumatettaa laatetta oyqqees.Qassikka ha adussa medhdhi xaafuwaassi keehin gita bila xifatiya deexoy assi de’ees. 
Olanchcha Kawoy   darin koyettenna maxaafa.I polo taarikiya boottaa mechchaa –Kaasaa Hayilu maarotinne qareti baynna  maataara de’iya izaawadan besettees . I ubba keehin busakkiya kawotettaa bollankk pheexi qezzees. Ay yohoynne, ubba,  I  an   mooraliyan woykko, kahan hashetuwan koyyiyaagaa  I be,ibeenna. Hagee tana 1066aan malatissidi xaafido  taarike maxaafa qommuwa hassayissees qassikka hegee ubbay :Taarikee kane  yootuwaakko saxetti shiiqida qofettiya woykko hassayettiya  haysetu   kasiya kaaluwa. I tumukka bila xifatiyaadan keehi koyettenna, yohuwan qassi  hagee taarikidankka  darin koyettenna. Yaatiyo gishshawu  A de’uwaakko ehanawu gidiya    awudee (context) woykko qonccisso gidenna.  Tumu lo’iya taarike maxaafaa woykko  cabbottiya mero taarike oottanawu  Tewodiroosa II denddoy  tumuka gidiya naqaashsha. Olanchcha Kawoy alamiya  metuwa nabbabuwaassi xaafettida Toophpheppe gidiya maxaaafa.
Daniachewu Worku  Oosota
Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa/ The Thirteenth Sun/(1973)
Taarikiya  kesuwan, Tammanne Heezzantta Away/ The Thirteenth Sun/ keehin keehin kawushsha. Keehin ceeggida piteweraariya Woldu na’aa Goytom, ba aawaa betidi biya asadan cima asay biidi ba sahuwaappe paaxiyoogaadan hidootiyo Zekuwaalla gadaamiyaakko mo’issiis. He sohuwa hemetaykka banqqatibeennaagaappe denddaagan Goytomi anhaa mooganawu ehiis. Oosoy, hemetaappe biidi  cima aawaa hayquwa gakkanaashin, naa”u gallassaappe guutta ekkiis, qassikka sohoy, biyo wodiyaaninne shaahettiyo wodiyan sarotettay gadaamiyaassi keehin mata  heera. Hanotay keehin undduwaallo, gidoppe attin gujo eeshshaawatuuninne sohuwa hanotaanne he wodiya hanotatuuna. Hagaa kasiya kaaluwan aatti yeggi goo’ettiyoogee, koyrottidi sohuwaaninne  wodiyan  wudin  keehin lo”o.
Zekuwaalli piddenna  tama xuussa hosppun woykko tammu mayliya haakkiya Adisaaba Bishoftuppe  xoqqa ogiya; loossuwaara kanttiyoogee keehin meto qassikka dere ba huuphen xoqqanne sitti giidi eqqidaagaa. Zekkuwaalla Abbossi geeyyidaagaa, keehin goyinettida Toophphiya  geeshshatussi,nne Abbo geeshsha haattaa, kireetere sima abbaa giyoogeeti  paxuwawu geeshshatu wolqqaa geetettees. Layttaa wodee Toophphiya Gifaata (September) aginan doommi qoodeettiya ooratta layttaa wodiyawu matattiyaagaa; hegeekka adussa medhdhi xaafuwa giddon denddida  zaari zaaridi  bukkiya wolqqaama iray agganaappe kasiyaana. Layttay mata; xaaifanchchay Zekkuwaalla xaafiiddi de’iiddi  daro wodiyawu simmi simmi xomoosiis.
Ha qatuwawu (Setting)  A huuphen  A garssan birshshettay de’iyoogaadan qofettees.Hagee meretaa pilggettaa, ayba sireekka daana danddayenna. Gidoppe attin  issi uri  hara birshshettaa demmanawu diggennaadan likketettaa xeellanawu paaciyara (tempitation) eqettiyaagaa gidana bessees. Amaaratto mooddee “xanna’ettida  qoncce gidenna( ambiguity) go’ettaara” gayttees;qassikka kawotu kawuwa, kallacchchaa  Toophphiyaanne geeshsha tama xuussaa giddon de’iya issimalatettaykka lo’o qaadadan gididoogee qoncce. Hagee hayyottiyoy odoy  A koyettiya metoy  deriya huuphphiyan de’iya eeshshaawatudan  gidenna;yohuwan qassiToophpheenne I dere asay Daynnaachchoy eta xeelliyoogaadaaninne eta hanotay( hagee ha’i wodiyan xaafuwan  ay ogiyaaninne  birshshettan danddayenna, ay maaraa naagida laamee  hanikkokka)’  Eeshshaawata pilggi paacciyoogee ha hayyuwa woykko qofaa kaafees.
Sahile Sillaaseppenne Dananaacho worqquppe simmin Inggilizettuwan xaafida hara xaafanchchay Abbe Gubegna gidishin A adussa medhdhi xaafuwa huuphe yohoykka Alemebeger / Defiance/(1975) Abbe  defiance /yuuqiyuuqenna/ giyaagee paashistte  Xaalee Toophphiya woraajjuwa  (1935-1941) zaari medhdhiya    taarikiyaawa woykko haydaawa  adussa medhdhi xaafo. Ha kasetidaageetuppe simmin  tishsha adussa  medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchati beettibookkona. 
Wotaaddara kawotettay wulli simmin, xinxxisuwan Inggilizettuwan xaafettida  Befeqaadu BekeleWolde Mariyaaman xaafettida Boottanne Zo’o shabbirssaabaa harinne haraashin zo’o shabbirssaabaa yootiya huuphe yohoy Maallado Guuran  Woruwa /Massacre  at Day Break/ (2003) demmoos. Ano eeshshaawati zo’o shabbirssaa maattaa uyidosona. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy yelaga asay ay keena he shabbirssatu harinne haraashin zo’o shabbirssaa maattaa uyidaakkonne bessanawu kajjeelees. He adussa medhdhi xaafuwa cuccumay polotikaakko baqqees.
Fiqire Marqqos Dasta Oosuwa (Works Of Fikire Maros Desta)
Adil”e Ciishsha  Milatiya Kormmaa Biittaa (Land of The Yellow Bull) 
1991aappe simmin , TDRP (EPRDF), wodiyan  Fikire Markos Dasti Kebusta Bestegerbanne  Evangaadi geetettiya ba adussa medhdhi xaafota Hamare asaa wogaanne de’uwa bessiya  Adil”e Ciishsha  Milatiya kormmaa Biittaa (Land of The Yellow Bull)/2003/  yaagiya  huuphe yohuwa birshshiis.  Hagee   asaa  sheeshshaa/ qommuwa/  (ethenographic novel) adussa  medhdhi xaafodan ekettees. Brittene biittan yelettidanne  ba deretettaa pilggettawu( social) harinne haraashin macca asatu de’uwan pilgganawu Toophphiya yiida qassikka wogaa dummatettaappe denddidaagan amarida  metoti gakkido Charlootee Ano eeshshaawiyo. Gidoppe attin,eeshshaawiya he deriya wogaaranne meeziyaara barina Hamere maccaasa gidaasu. A Hamare goobaa Deltti Gelddiira siiquwan wullawusu. Hegaappe guyyiyan  A Hamare maccaasay azinaa gelanawu kunttiyo ubbabaa kunttada  A gelaasu meezeyanawu nookkaasu. Wodiyaappe guyyiyan A he dere asaanne eta wogaa dosada.
Adussa medhdhi xaafuwa giddon issi uri keehin lo’iya eeshshawatunne qatotu qonccissota  xeellana danddayees. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy Inggilizettuwan Toophphiya asan  xaafettida hara ay bila xifatiya oosuwan beettenna  dumma deretettaa ( unique society) bessees.
Ha garssaara de’iya garxxi ekkido nibaabee  he Adussa medhdhi xaafuwaappe ekettidaagaa. Hegeekka ano eeshshaawaa  Charlotta qonccissiyaagaa 
Bollaa meecettiyo kifiliyan, issi maccaasiya keehin ciimman shemppawusu, ba shempuwaakka bombbaappe wodhdhiya haattaa cenggurssaadan carqqattada  haatturawusu. Haattaa ganday baggan kumiis.  Charloota adussan  haatta garssi yeddada  ba  ushachcha gediya haattaa ganddaa miyyiyaakko yeddada matan de’iya  penttissiyo gaaniya  xanna’aasu. Haattaa ganddawu ushachcha miyyiyan, kushe sayiniyaappe bolla baggaara, de’iyaagee  xaazan kumida heregaa. Penggiyawu haddirssa  miyyiyaara ubbaykka ibaa gidiya, qita t-sharttetun,bolaaletuuninne shooqa jaakkeetatun kumidi eqqida zambbillee de’ees. Appe qommo baggaara, A bollan bootta woyni xajje alleeqido pooxay kaqettiis. Kifiliya xuuntta gidikkonne ,  I geeshshaanne keehin lo’iyaagaa.  Charloota  issitoo issitoo ba  zareta oychchaasu. Gidoppe attin, ha’i A  ba gaytotettaa Steebe Martinaara sinttawu suganaakko agganaakko  giyoogan  haddira uttaasu. A ganddaa giddo  haattaa melissada bollaa mecettiyoosawu simmaasu, hagee qassi I  shugo bootta bollaa bollan pushakettidi duge simmidi goggees. I qantta gurdee Ishugo ikissiya/huuphphiya/, karettanne bootta bollaa xi’issiyo pooxaara  bolla  baqqi oyqqiis. I worqqa  xaatta huuphee I zokkuwaaranne I tiraara oyqettiis. I huuphphiyaappe duge wodhdhiya haattay Ideemuwa musul”issiis qassikka I ayfiya lacuwaa irxxissiis.  Haattaa irxxay I  naa”u shugo molaala shaaho tiraara duge hemettiyoogaa dommiis.  A de’iyoosay  ho’uwaappe kiyida cuwan kamettiis, hegeekka qassi keehin meeggiya guuran maataa bollan de’iya  xaazaa tizitaa. 
Charlloota, guuliyan kamettida heregaakko shiiqada ba daabidaaba misiliya xeellaasu. Ba misiliya disennan ixxada ba xanttata siiqaasu. A ba ushachcha xanttaa ba ushachcha kushiyan oyqqiyoode, I haddirssaagee  hankko bollaa shaahuwaakko goshettidi wodhdhees. A  I kushshiya xeeray awan eqqidaakko xanna’aasu. 
Aaho boottanne bunnaama magalasho gidikkonne, aadhdhiya kaamiya cenggurssay haahuwaara guurummees.  Mentte hiittatu gidduwan, hiitta miyye xomppee xaraphpheezzaa bollan uttiis.  Xomppiya kaallidi  iraadiya kaaseetee “SOONIYA” zal”e malaataara naa”u xeetu layttaappe kase xaafettida Mozartte piano sonata kaa’iis. Maskkootiya lanqqiyan  de’iya naa”u  qeeri xaraphpheezzatu bollan  xaaramussiyaassi baggan de’iya eessan mal”ettido toophphiya heera ( traditional) haraqee eqqiis.

                                                                                       (Land of the yellow Bull:pp 19-20)
Fiqire Markoosi ba adussa medhdhi xaafotun ehiidobay eeshaawatu qonccissota . I keehin minnidi eeshshaawatu misiliyaanne oosota qonccissiis. Amarida eeshshaawatu qonccissoti taarikiya qaattaa teqqikkonne, A mule odoti yootiyoogaappe bessiyo hiillaa bollan wudoosona.  Qonccissoti nabbabiyaageeti banttarkka eeshshaawatu oosotanne misileta  be’anaadan oottees. Gidikkonne, I issitoo issitoo maayetuwan haasayaanne oduwa go’ettiyo bilaa eraa xayees, woykko ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy issoy issuwaara gayttennaagaa gidees.Issitoo issitoo keehi koshshenna oosotussi daro paatettata immiyo metoti de’oosona. Oosoti ubbatoo wodiyaanne sohuwa moosona. Hagee Adil”e Ciishsha  Milatiya Kormmaa Biittaa (Land of The Yellow Bull)  giddon qoncciyan beettees.
Hara Amaarattuwaappe Inggilizettuwawu  birshshettida adussa medhdhi xaafoy  Yismake Worku Dertogada(2012) yaagiyo Zelaaleme Niguisen  birshshettidaagaa. Issi baggaara, ha adussa medhdhi xaafuwa Amaaratto birshshettay xaaxi waaxuwan nabbabiyaageetu lannqqiyan keehin ekettidaagaanne  qassikka zaari zaari attamettidaagaa. Hagee qantta wodiyan daro koppetun attamettida Amaaratto adussa medhdhi xaafotuppe issuwa gidanne danddayees. Issi baggaara, Yoftahe Seyoum (Phd) adussa medhdhi xaafuwa  kaseyuwan, “Derttogadawu  kaseyuwa”yaagiyoogan bari  hayyuwa  immees. A shaahuwaappe amaridaagee ha kaalliyaagaadan nabbabettees. 
Sinttata eesuwan poga simmada, qaalata doora simmada, oduwaassi xinxxiso qofata akeek simmada, Ta ta huuphen Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafoy,hegeekka  ciimma xiskkuwan haatturiyoogaappe aadhdhiyaagee,wurssettan ha’i wodiyan beegottiis. Bila eratettaaninne meruwan yelaga eranchchaa Yismake Worqqun xaafettida  Derttogaadi (Dertogada)  issi oyshi baynnan Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafuwa oosotu zawaa  qolchchi beettanaadan oottiis. Ta un”uwaassi( worry) pultto gidiyaagee xaafanchchaa woykko harabaa gidenna nabbabiyaageetappe attin. Eti keehin ufayssiyaanne A dumma maxaafaa bollan xekkaappe wodhdhidaba gaana danddayiyo hayyotussi cashshaa guytiyan  tana  ufayissibookkona. Gidoppe attin,ayi! Ta hanno gakkanaashin Derttogaada oosuwa bollan co’u giikke. Ay payyatettaara de’iya (sane) nabbabiyaagee issi siree baynnan pudenne duge wotti xeellidi xaafanchchawu A cora taariketussi  gatiya immidi Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafuwa hiddaasiyaakko ayfiya olana. Derttogadi ha’inne sintta yeletawu imettida dumma imota giyoogee koshshenna. 
Issi uri Derttogadi giddo (average) Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafuwa likkiyaappe aadhdhanaadan sugiya qaalan qonccettenna eeshshatuppe guutta giishin amaridaagaa taani ziiriyan wottanaagaa naagana bessees. Doommishin, taarikiyawu baaso kaalatoy dumma.  Maxaafaa garssan qonccettida, yootettidanne aahuwan phoolettida qofay hara Toophphiya xaafanchchatun boshettibeenna. Hara baggaara oosuwan bessiyaageetinne(actors) beegotissiyaagee kahaappe ubba wodeti aadhdhinkka  qucettanawu meto. I ajjuuta gido. 
Bila xifatiya oosuwaassi dumma wuday imettidaba gidikkonne, kase xaafettida  Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa (The Thirteenth Sun) nne Aferssaata milatiya  adussa medhdhi xaafuwaara annaacissanawu  meto. Gidikkone, assi A hummunnatettan woykko murutatettan  gatee imettana bessees.  Tumukka, I ba wodiyan  Toophphiyan de’iya naa"u Inggilizetto doona medhdhi xaafotuppe issuwa.
Hara Inggilizettuwan  xifattida bila xifatiya  oosoti Haile Mariaama Solomona, Yelaga  Zammaachchiya/ The young Crusader/ (2011), Ayele Gebayo Kessi Ekuwa/ Escape/(2011), nne Tekilemaariyaama Meeroni, Dabbiddaabiya/The Letters/(2011). Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoti COD Toophphiya yaagiyoogee Xaafanchchatu annaaciyaa  Woytuwa bila xifatiya annaaciyawu   giigissido  maaduwan  xaafettidosona.
Xaaxi waaxuwan, Inggillizettuwan xaafettida adussa medhdhi xaafoy qoodan cora gidenna. Sahile sillaase Afersaataa/Afersata/(1967),Olanchcha kawuwa/The Warier King/(1974),nne Tama Mittaa /The Fire Brand/ (1979), giyo adussa medhdhi xaafoti Afirkkaa xaafanchchatu mazggabaa garssan de’oosona. Hara adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchatuura  annaacissiyoode daro adussa medhdhi xaafota Inggillizettuwan I xaafidoogaadan  mazggabay A kushshiyan de’ees. Ba bila era hummunnatettan woykko murutatettan (qualities) keehin  lo”o adussa medhdhi xaafodan  xeelettiya hara adussa medhdhi xaafoy, Workku dannachcho, Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa/ The Thirteenth Sun/(1973) yaagiyoogaa. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoti Toophphiya bila xifateti Inggilizettuwan yelettiyo wodiyan xaafettidanne attamettida adussa medhdhi xaafota. Daro layttaassi  hara adussa medhdhi xaafoti Toophphiya Diyasppora bil xifatiyan beettana gakkanaashin. Tumukka,Amaarattuwaappe Inggilizettuwawu birshshettida Dastta Fiqire Marqqoosa,Adil”e  Ciishsha Milatiya kormmaa biittaa/ Land of The yellow Bull(2003), nne Worqqu Yismaakke Derttogada( dertogada) milatiya   adussa medhdhi xaafoti de”oosona. Hara  koyro kochchoorokka Inggilizettuwan xaafettida adussa medhdhi xaafoti Ayele Gebayu,Kessi ekuwa/Scape/(2012), HayileMaariyaam Solomona,Yelaga Zamaachchaa/TheYoung Crusade/nne Tekile Maariyaama Meeroni, Dabiddaabiya/ The Letters/,(2012). Ha adussa medhdhi xaafoti yelaga Toophphiya tamaaretussi, harinne haraashin naa”antto xekkaa timirtte keettaa tamaaretussi xaafettidaageeta. 
1.2.2.3. Qantta Taarkiya qommotanne Qantta Taarikiya xaafachchata
Haraara gatti xeelliyoogan generee/qommoy, qantta taarikee murutettiyoogaa woykko xaafettidi kiyiyoogaa xeelliyaagan keehin guutta. Ha’i wodiyan, issi uri doorettida  heezzu   qantta taarikiya maxaafatu xallaa demmees. Etappe naa’’ay koyro kochchooruwan Inggilizettuwan xaafettiis, qassi heezzanttoogee Amarattuwaappe inggilizettuwawu birshshettidaagaa. Ha oosoti 10 qantta taariketa(adussa qantta taariketa),Hayilu Alamu Sugo Karameellaa/Fondant/(Wolddayinnuwa woykko danttuwaanne yeda medhdhi xaafuwa)nne 20 qantta taariketa oyqqiya Maammo Seefu Keehin Laaqunttiya  Qantta Taarikiyaageeta (Fascinating Short Stories).  Haray qassi G/ Igzi’aabeeraa  Samaate Amaaratto  danttuwaappe birshshettida Zerettaa (Thee Seed) yaagiyoogaa.
Hageetu bollan gujuwan, hara Ingilizettuwaappe birshshettida woykko koyro kochchoorokka  Inggilizettuwan xaafettid Inggilizettuwan  tumudan birshshettida  Libeena  Tadessa  Lunet  giyoogaa milatiya  qantta medhdhi xaafoti de’oosona.  Hagee Lunet yaagiyoogee  Yeguleelawu Sekaraamee beettanaashin  koyro  zammaana Amaaratto Qantta Taarikedan xeellettees.  Hara baggaara, gaazeexatuuninne magazeenetun  attamettida amarida qantta taariketi de’oosona.  Kabbada Ashenafen xaafettida  Manyahilishalisa bullachchaykka  qantta taariketuppe issuwa. Hageekka, ha moojuuliya giddon nabbabettanawunne laalettanawu  gelliis. 
Ha kaalliya qantta taarikiya  loytti wudi nabbabidi akeekanawu kajjeelite.
Manyahlishala bullachchaa
Kabbada Ashennaafen.
Ha bullachchay polettidoy  Gifaata  aginan 1926  issi gallassaana. Gelettanawunne naati yelettanawu, I 22attan pee’iya, kumetta paydo gidiya, lo”o qaadaa malaatiya, poo’o  Wogga (Sunday). Mushuriya, layttay 13 gidiyo kawee Zawuditi Kawo garuwa naagiyaagaa na’iyo, Manyhahlishaalo. Mushuray qassi wambbettiyaa sheeshsha( nobleman) gidiya  qassikka ba “cima ayfe imenna”( “fruitless”) machchiyo birshshanawunne ha na’aa yelanawu qaalaa gelida  na’iyo, Manyhahlishaalo ekkanawu  maacida, layttay 30 gidiyo Haymaanoota Takila. Takilee birshshanaadan denttettida  hara gita koshshiya  gaasoy de’ees. A 32 layttaa oyqqida machchee galbbay keehin karetta qassikka I sinttay iitees.  Issi ayba puulikka baawa, ha  worqqa Toophphiya galbbi baawa, issi he lee’enne yeemoyiya menttershshi baawa, issi kozoza siireenne  I  ba  mala wambbetto sheeshshawu bessiya maccaasaappe naagiyoone qofan be’iyo sululla bolli  issi baawa.
Qanttan, Manyahlishala,naagidoogaappe aaro puula. Inne A akase aawati  bantta huuphen O machchodan dooridoogawu ufayttidoToophphiya wombbeto ( noble) puulatanne hummunnatettaa ubbaa  A oyqqaasu.  Tumukka,  Takilee  ba giigissido mushure layttassi  keehin un”ettiis. Gidikkonne, I ba huuphiyaanne ba hayqqida aawaa ayyaanaa ufayissanawu  ooso tangguwa ekkanawu koshshiis. I Manyahlishalo azinadaaninne aawadan O de’uwa ogiya tamaarissanawu ekkana koshshiis. Yaatiyo gishshawu, 13 tta layttan, Manyahlishala  ha 30u  layttaawa  izaawuura gelettiyo ekettiyoogan qaphi gaasu. A ba azinaabaa eriyo issiba kanchchee assi wombbeto (noble) yeletay de’iyoogaa. A ubba A wombbetetto(nobility) hummnnatettaa, woykko keenaanne meraakka eriyoobi baawa.   A issibaa eranaadan oottiyaakko lo’oshin attiis. Mushuray issi sinttay keehin aleeqido baluquwa bollan  uttidi seeta awan  biis. Mushuray  ba doorettida asata  matan kaallidi sebban kumidi dunkkaaniyaakko geliis. A ajjaabeti ( dooddiyaageeti)/ Escots/ qoodan 40 aappe bolla. Ubbaykka banttassi giigida sohuwan uttidosona. Mushuriya puttu gaasu. Hegaappe simmin sirphphatettay dariis. Ubbaykka boottaa maayuwa  maayidosona. Manyahlishala ba de’iyoosaappe doorettida  mushuraa asatun dunkkaaniyaakko yaasu. O  kaallidi macca . miizeti ( bride maids) gelidosona.  A  asa ayifettenna mala onikka I sinttaa be’ana danddayibeenna. Mushuraynne A imattati ubbay A uttana gakkanashin eqqidosona. Hegaappe simmin,ubbaykka bantta kushiya baqqidi bantta oydiyaakko simmidosona. Bonchcho diggisee-Ushshati……qiraariya, xajjiya qumati ……Woxiyaa, buddeenaa, qaye ashuwa michchiya barbbariyara . Durssay-naachchay. Oh! Ayiba ufayissiyaabee!Wodee paalliis. Awa ayfee  wullanawu matiis.  Dunkkaaniyaaanne  duriyaageetu gaxa kiyi beettiya kuway dunkkaaniya penggiyaara  beettiis. Biyo wodee gakkiis. Dorettida heezzu asati denddidi eti baanaassi bolluwaa A lo”o   sheniya oyichchidosona. Ha cima aaway ba imatuwa aduqissana koyyikkonne, eta heekettaaassi (insistence)  giidi sohuwa immiis. Eta baanaadan koshshees giis.
Mushuree aawaynne dabboti attin  hara ubbay denddiis. Haranttuwaakka co’atettay(silence) dariis. A amarida daqiiqaassi  baawaakko simmada  A tohuwa sinttan gulbbataasu. A ba garbbaliya ziqqi oottada   I  ha geluwa ekuwa/ marriage) anjjanaadan  A wogga buhiya maayi uttida gediya yeraasu.  A ba woossiyoobawu ayba qofaa hinttee baynnan de’ishiina. A hegaa oottanaassi kasetada yootana bessawusu .  Hegeeti eko gelossi ammano maarata. A anjjoy O tumu awan I omarssaa   peeshanaakko A ayibakka erabeykku.  Hiyyeesa Manyahlishala. A  erukku! I  aawaa ayfeti afuttan musul”idosona. I xeellidi ba qiiba na’iyo meezetibeenna imata uraassi agganaagee assi keehin deexxiis. Gidoppe attin, hegee haniyoogee attennaba gidiis.  Hageeti de’o ogeta. I anjjota  issi immidi  wurssetta mo’isso yeruwa O yeriis.  Manyahlishala siiphphotayidda denddada bana  imattaa zokkuwan demmaasu. A imattaa dunkkaaniyaappe efaydda de’awusu, woykko qassi imatay  eeno giidinne minnidi barkka bana  baluquwaadan laaggiiddi de’ees.  I wodiratinne gedeti A xeessaassi issi bagga miyyiyaara  kaqettidi gooli gooliiddi de’oosona.  Garssa baggaara A kushee I deexuwa kaafiis. A qoncciyan A ayfiya  be’ukku asa ayfiya gishshataassi. A  eti  “keehin lo”o asa” giidoogaadankka, tuma gaada ekkaasu. Hagee keehin lo”o asati poliyo ooso qommo.  A qassikka  I  O  A  diccido  I aawaasooppe ehidoogaa eraasu qassikka  Bana wurssettan mushuraaso ehida baluqiyookka  dosaasu. Isoy imatta soho gidiis. Takile aayee imattati naa’u mushurata  penggeppe  mokki ekkidosona. Ashkarati woxxi yiidi dorettida asati O baluquwaappe wodhdhanawu maaddishin  paraa bixaalaa oyqqidosona. Curqqa maayuwa maayida banttassi coo  ogiyaara  aadhdhiya asati  hanettiyaaba  ufayttiiddi eqqidi xeellidosona. Amaridaageeti bantta kushshiya baqqidosona haraati qassi cenggurssaa xoqqu oottidi miiccidosona. Shooron de’iya attuma naati, shamize xallaa maayidi,ufayissa baalaa be’idi markkattanawu shiiqidosona.Haray atto  kanatikka guyyenne sinttawu  galjjidabaadan   baluquwaa bollaaninne issoy issuwa bollan  bocciiddi  woxxidosona. Hegaappe guyyiyan ubbaykka dunkkaaniya giddo gelidosona.Manyahlishala ba bolloten kaaletettada, haranttuwa hokkaydda bana demmawusu,anjjuwaassinne dosetuwaassi (acceptance) woossanawu I menttershshati imattee buhe tohuwa  bollan tokettidosona.Bollotiya Manyahlishalo sa’aappe denttada I sinttaa qaaraasu. Naa”anttuwan,na’ee puulatettaa malaaluwaaninne I galbbaa shom”atettan omooddettaasu. Gidoppe attin,mataarakka   ixxayddanne  qanaataydda  I ayfetun beettaasu. “Taani gelettiyo wode idan pula gidikke,” yaagada qoppaasu. I kushee Manyahlishali hashiya bollan guuttaa kokkoriis.  Manyahlishala hegee issi siyettin  ba bollotee  ayfiya demmanawu pude xoqqu gaasu. He ayfeti “  Ne pula gidikkonne ta na’aa kushiyan wulladasa giyaaba milatoosona. Puulatettay hegaa xalla gidenna. Attuma asay dosiyo hara hummunatettay( quality) de’ees.  Ta ne kunddiyoogaadan hidootayis. Ne hachchi omarssi  barchchetiyoogaadan hidootayiis. Ta nena ne barchchiya gatiyan ta na’a xallay  ufayttanaassi anjjana.”I bollotiya hegaappe guyyiyan sinttaa poo’issada O anjjaasu. 
He bullachcha gallasaa shoraappe (eve) doommin,  mushuriya,Manyahlishala attin asa ubbay keehin ufayttiis.  Ufayissa cenggurssay imbbilttatuppe kiyees. Kushee issoy issuwaara qanxxennan  xarphphattees. Bollay  ufayissaaninne hombbocuwan  karaabiya eeduwaara kikikattees. Ee, hagee  Manyahlishali bullachcha gallasaa shoraa (eve). Gidikkonne,ubba asay, I aawaakka gujjin, issi, mushureessi, miyoobaa immiyoogaa, dogidosona. A qumaa oychchabeykku.Hegee mushuri  oottiyooba gidenna. A Hegaadan oottikko hegee  muleera pokko. Issi sha’u  ganjjiyaassi gidiya qumay son de’ees, gidoppe attin, A, mushuriya mushura gidenna asaadan, namisaappe denddaagan  barka yeekkaydda, karchchiya mela gonffay qaaterettido elunchchaara bana xiskkuwan olaasu. Kaalliya guuran,gallassinne,omarssi keehin qiibabay issi manaassi imettiis. Ubba hegan issi ba kushiya go’ettanawu shenee imettibeenna. A amarida barssota ba  muuzetun  maadettaasu. Issi issi daqiiqan cuullees. A daafuraasu.  A he gallassay aadhdhanaagaa ay keeni amottadeeshsha. A  ay keeni  laamotadeenne woossadee  he ufayissiya  asay shiiqidosaappe barina shaakkiyo qaadaa demmanawu ! Barkka gidanawu . Barkka xiskkanawu.
Wurssettan, qammaappe usuppun saatiyawu shiiqiiddi de’ees . Keehin koshshiya wodee, ubbakka sirphpha malay, wurssettay, baalaa diggissiyaassi xeera zaway. Karaabiya baqay wurssettay gakkanashin , ubbaykka, shoollaqidosonanne cuuridosona.Asay ooratta  hanotan dooyettida qooriyan miidosonanne uyidoson . Eti qassikka hagaa gaanawu danddayettenna heennan(enthusiasm) duridosona. Amaridaageeti qassi heennan kumidi bantta cenggursaa keehin xoqqissidi haasayidosona. Haraati qassi  bantta cenggurssa xoqqissidi ha’i ha’i miiccidosona.  Daro caway mushuraassi som”uwaara duuge simmidi xoohiis. I keehin un”ettiis.   Gallassa kumettaa I uyin  A be’a erennaagaappe daruwa uyiis.  burccukkoy zaari zaaridikka haraqiyan kumiis.  I mino ushshaa zaari zaari uyiyoogee assi lo”o gidiyoogaadan  hayyottidi   doorettida asi ( the best man)  A  minttettiis, A hegee  maaddiyoogaadan.  Koyro kuttoy waassiis.  Giddo qammaa ( mid night). Xeeraa gakkiis ( The climax). Mushuriyaanne mushuray hiitta kifiliyaakko gelidosona.  Doorettida  asi mushuray maayuwa kessanaadan maaddiis. Hegaadankka, mushuriyookka I doorettida muuziya (bridesmaids)  maaddaasu. Hegaappe guyyiyan naa”u keettayiyaanne keettaaway ( couples) gayttanawu banttarkka attidosona( issi issi qaalaa hennan) . Mushuray  amarida yasha woosa mala qaalata haasayiis. Hegaappe simmin,  I issi siiquwaassi oottiyo   woosa malabaakka hanotan bessiis. Hegee, gidikkonne,  musureeppe ayba zaarokka xayiis. Hiyyeesa Manyahlishala kiitaappe bagga meretan demmaasu; I ay oychchiiddi de’iyaakko akeekaasu.   I  A  wolqaamatettaanne  A  xunchchaa  bonchchada qassikka  attumatettaa aagaa bonchcha maaddada saruwan I oottana bessanawu  A assi eeno gaana mala koyyiis.  Eesuwaara! “Ta otta gade gidiyoogaa  I dogideeyee?A qoppaasu.”Hagee keehin   sakkiyaabee?” Hegaappe guyyiyan, A muleera assi haalluuti gaada ixxaasu. “Ta doorettida asappe  taassi ayba maaddoykka yeena,”Mushuray maaciis. I hassayennan,xalaaninne yiilluwan kumidi A  hiittan zin”ida zozzu ga ixxida na’ekko simmiaggiis. I maayuwa  pooshshi olinneekka I huuphiyaara gattidi O oyqqi aggiis. A  mino kushshiyaappe kessa ekkana giyo baaxiyan ba adussa xugunttata A ashuwaa garssi colttu oottada yeddaaggaasu. Yohoy denddiis.  Suutta be’oy! Sahuwaappe denddaagan bitaniya  waasoy! Gidoppe attin mataarakka Manyahlishalaala  siiqo hanqquwan tucetti xuuqqanaaniya  aara kum”u gaaggaasu.  A mino kushetuppe yiya shochchay I kushetunne  daalletu  dibbata donjjillissi oliyaaggiis. Cawaa! Ooliya!Daro cawaa! Daro ooleta!  Akka  issi sakkiyaaby simbbiriiddi I garssaara  canttiyoogaa  akeekaasu. Shemppuwa balido dagama waasoy waasettiis!  Ikka kayyiya   demmido shemppuwa  sheenuqiiddi  ha’i ha’i yeddiis. Oosoy  oosettiis. Takilee, mushuray, ayyiiddi denddidi maayuwa  maayiis. I ba mushureeninne  banan ufayttiis.
A doorettida  asi  mishiraachchuwa  naagiya imattatussi erissiis. “ Daro  ushshay bonchchettida godatussi! Muuzunqqaa kaa’iya asay mushuriyo sabbona(galatona). Mushuriya  bazzon de’iya woran de’iya  sulqqisulqqiya  orooze(rose) cishshaa mala.  Muuzunqqaa kaa’iya asay mushuraa sabbona(galatona). Eti A wolqqaama  attumatettawunne   goobatettawu  yexxona. I zeeridi ba zerettaa otta biittan zeriis! I  A attumatetta wolqqaa  paacciyo paaciya bonchchuwan aadhdhiis. 
1.2.2.4. Diraamaanne diraamaa oottiyaageeta(Drama and dramatist) /plays and playwrights)
Meeziya-7 
Kaalliya oyshata citan gididi zaarite 
1.Toophphiyan Inggilizetto diraamay koyro oonan doommidee ereeti?
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2. Ane Tsaggaaye G/ Mediini xaafido ingglizetto draamatussi  issi heezzaa gidiya huuphe yohota  xaafite. 
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
Amaarattonne  Inggilizetto doonatun Toophphiyan diraamaa taarikee  issi bizza izaawuura keehin oyqettidi  beettees. Dummatettan wottiyoode, Toophphiya diraamay Inggilizettuwan ba yeletaanne dichchaa daruwa xaafidanne  deree kushshiya baqqido tiyaatiriya xaafanchchaa  woytettida bonchcho G/ Mediina Tsaggaayeera gattees. I barkka gaana danddayiyo hanotan  1951 doommidi  issi xeetu layttawu  bagga wodiyaappe aadhdhana gakkanaashin  misiliyan  bollatettan beettiis. A erettida Ingglizetto kaassatuppe ( ha’i wode pilgganchchaa erissana gakkanaashin), Yexissiyaagaa( Azimari), Oda Oak Ooracle, Tewodiroosa( ubbaykka 1965), nne Yarshsho buquraa  dom”ettaa / Collision of Altars/(1971xaafettidi 1977 attamettiis). Wurssettaagee  daro doonatun birshshettidi dumma dumma kare biittatun  be’ettiis. Inggillizetto doonan hara diraamaa oosoy Gubaynna Abeben(  hachchi gakkanaashin geelladan barkka naa”antto tiyatiriya xaafanchchaa) xaafettidanne 1964  merettida Makkala  Na’iyo/ The Savage Girl/ giyoogaa.  
Haraara gatti xeelliyoode, Diraamaa xaafettay( nabbabo xalla diraamay)/ Closet diraama/, Toophphiya bila xifatiyan  Inggilizetto  diraaman leppi beettees.
 1.3. Toophphiya Inggilizetto bila xifatiyawu ano cuccumata 
 Bantta Amaaratto   oosotun keehin erettida   cora Toophphiya xaafanchchati   qassikka Inggilizetto adussa medhdhi xaafoti, kaassatinne danttoti attamettidosona. Hegeekka geelladan eratettaa meezetanaassa (intellectual exercise) woykko nabbabiyaageeta corayanaassa /woykko  Amaarattuwa  dirssaatuppe la’a kessanaassa. 
1.3.1.   Taarikiyaawa  adussa Medhdhi Xaafota (Historical Novels)
Meeziya-8
Ane  kasetidi kaalliya oyshata  citan gididi  zaarite
1. Ane intte eriyo taarikiyaawa adussa medhdhi xaafota xaafite
________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2. Taarikiyaawa adussa medhdhi xaafota xaafida Toophphiya xaafanchchatuppe intte eriyoogeeta xeesite
________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
Sahile Sellaase Olanchcha Kawuwa/ The Warior King/ (1974) 18tta xeetu laytta   Toophphiya deretettanne polotikaa moottaa  hanotan  puttu giida  Tewodiroosa giddooninne  sunttettida  mokkaaninttetunne qeesetu  giddon de’iya  maataa (power) baaxiya  qonccissidi bessees. Olanchcha Kawoy Tewodiroosa II dendduwa paattidi yootiya 18tta xeetu layttaa  Toophphiya polotikkaa moottan naa”u gita qofatuura-kumetta Toophphiya walakki issua oottiyoogaanne  zammaanatettaa. Hageekka dariya baggi   issippe gididi eqettiya cora qeesetu baaxiyaara   eqettanaassa.  Tewodiroossi daro adussa medhdhi xaafotinne kaassati pulttodan ammanettiyo  deree kushiya baqqido asa.
 Taarikiya layttatu kasiya kaaluwa naagida plootiya/plot/ quxaroy laaletta Zemene Mesaafintte Tewodiroosa kallachcha xallaa gakkanaashin zardda’ees. Amarida taarikiya eranchchati  Tewodiroosi ajjuutan yelettida 200 layttaa  ba wodiyaappe  sinttatidaagaa yaagoson. 
Haray guutta gomppay de’iyo  Sahile Sellaasen xaafettida  Huuphe yohoy Aferssaataa /Afersata/ (1969) giyoogee  Toophphiya meeze  eqotan danuwa pilggettaappe simmin  sunttettiis. I dariya baggi pilggetta  adussa medhdhi xaafuwa milatiyaaba gidikkonne, assi  daro malalalettiyoobay paca qassikka he pilggetta mdhdhi xafuwa hanotaa carkkuwan ashi aggees. Taarikiyaassi koshshiya yohoy  issi Guraage shuchchan keettaa xuussaa hegeekka  haysiyan  sirettidaagaa  meeze pilggetta ogetun  pilliqiyoogaa.
1.3.2. Polotikaa Boriya
 He xaafanchchankka xaafettidaTama Mittaykka /The Fire Brands/(1979) Xuusaappe kase Toophphiya magaanxxo simeretuwa bollan wudiya  polotikaara gayttidaba. Hagee  kawushshan guuttaa xaafido adussa medhdhi xaafo. DayinnaachchoTammanne Heezzantta Away/ The Thirteenth Sun/(1973) xuussappe kase Toophphiya  issippetettaanne Ikkoonome hanotatun wudiya mino bore. 
Debebe (1980:609-624)   wottiyoogaadan  hagee  kawushshan  guuttaa  xaafido  adussa medhdhi xaafo. Hegaa gishshawu  hargganchcha pitiraaree  ba naatun  xomoosettidi (Goyitomanne Woynito)   Zikula deriyan de’iya  Abbo geeshsha sohuwa payyatettaa kaallanawu   biyoogaa  doommiis. pitiraaree buuraanne dembbaa  kanttidi  geeshshaa sohuwa  biidi bana  bonchchuan kaalliyaageetuura  issi goshshanchcha  keettatun   shemppiis.  Goshshanchchaa machchiya  meeze (traditional) maataawatussinne  daggamiyaageetussi  eraa immiya shareechcho maccaasa.  Gujuwankka, ubba haattay, pitiraaree shareechcho maccaaseekko  paxana giidi  bees.  Hegee haniiddi de’ishin, koyruwaappe doommidi Woinito xeelliiddi de’iyaagee wurssetta gallassan O tunissiis/ mooriis/. Pitiraaree ba na’iya mooretuwaassi ( rape) aatta imettidoogaa demmidaagee, goshanchchaa  keehin qamman markkinne  naqaashi erettennan wori simmidi bawukka hayqqees. Adussa  medhdhi xaafuwawu huuphe yohoy hachchi gakkanaashin de’iya  kase Toophphiya zannaqqa dirjjitiya erisso postteriyaappe  mucurin  ekkettidaagaa. 
Beautiful Ethiopia! Thirteen months of sunshine!
Smock Nyala!Smock Kitelework!
Adussa medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchati keehin naanida xuussaappe kase Toophphiya huqqunnaanne maganxxuwa qaran kumidi ( skillfully)  bessoosona.Tumukka, Tammanne heezzau aginatu  awa ayfee  baceessuwan ( ironically) tammanne heezzu aginatu xumaa malaatees, hiyyeesatettaa( penury), namisaa, yeellaa woykko kawushshaa.
 Imatta  gidiya tammanne heezzu agina goshshanchchati   Toophphiya  deree  kanttido kallachchaa kawotettaa (monarchy)  boxooxissiyaageetanne  sikkina xumaa gishshatiyaageeta. 
Hiillatettan, Taye ( 1980:739) hegee kunddettaa misiliyoogaadan  qonccissees. Misilee ciimmayidi akeekiyo mereta xeeluwaa( visual) , sissaa( auditory),nne  singgiyoogaa (olfactory)-  qasssikka gunddatettaa, maganxxuwa,yeletaa mooriyoogaa, gilqqatetta pulttissees. Bantta ha’i wode   misiletu meecettay  leemisuwaassi   Pultto haattay, geeshsha haattay, iray, di’oy, dada gunttay,  bawuta do’ata diggiyoogee, nne  tamaa xuussay  panddaa meechchay xinqqiya musabaa diggiyoogawu waannabaTaye(1980:747) . Teklu(1983),giyoogaadan Dagnachon xaafettida Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa /The Thirteenth Sun)  attamoy  Toophphiya adussa medhdhi xaafo bila oosuwa hiillan kantti kiyidi  kaalettiis. 
Kaalliya  malaatati koshshiyaageeta.
1.Geeshsha sohuwaakko biyoogaa (The pilgrimage)- Toophphee la’a kiyanaadan koyyiyoogaa malaatees.
2. Pitiraariya ( Fitawrari)- Piudaale iita  sugettaa malaatees.
3. Zikkuwaalla (Zikwala) - Ubaa wokaliyaagaa woykko  biittee  xuussaa ( revolution) shoraa  ubbaa malaatees. 
4. Woynito( Wointu)- Piudale  dannatinne  goshshanchchati dosiyo( issi woossiyo) Toophphiyo malaatees.
Taya (1980)  nne Debeba(1986) doonay I  barkka baassi wudaa immiyoogaan cuccumaa( theme)  genttees yaagidi palamoosona. Ay liketuwankka , ay xekkankka I erettida adussa medhdhi xaafo. Taye ( 1980:747) / David F, Beer be’a / “ Toophphiya Inggilizetto mero xuufiya gomppatanne pulttota,”Afirkkaa bila xifatiya pilggettaa,gom.8.pd.1.1977(sin.99-124) .  Abbea yuuqiyuuqenna /Defiance/( 1975) giyoogee  paashistte Toophphiya woraajjuwa( 1935-41) zaari medhdhiya taarikiyaawa  adussa medhdhi xaafo.
Aduwaa muttumuroy karetta sheeshshi Awurooppaa paashisttiya bollan xoonuwa qumaayido malaata xoonuwa geetettees woykko lancciya Awurooppaa haaro maataawatu Awurooppaa-Afirkkaa dom”ettaassi  simo zawadan hassayettees.  Hegaa gishshawu,  Xaalee  oytamu layttata kumettaa wotaaddara wolqqaa keehin bobboxissidi 1928 M.L. Toophphiya bollan denddis. Hegeekka oyqqiyo wodiya (1928-1933 M.L) geetetti erettees. Sooninne karen Wotaaddaranne gaannatetto  baaxetuwaappe  haraa  issippetettaa  kawotettawu (league of nations) maganay oosettiis.  Hegee haniiddi de’ishin Giraazinen kaaletettiya Paashistte  wotaaddaray wolqqan xaliyoo ( rapping)  oosuwa  Addisaaban  wolqqan xaliyo( rapping) oosuwaappe biidi busakko olaa gakkanashin   deriyaa  maraara shukkiis.
Abbee ha taarike oosuwa  koora baaxiya ogiya oyttiiddi  izaawatuppe –izaawatun  naagettiyaabaaninne amarida haariyaageeta wokkaliyaageetinne  arbbayinnati  baaxetidosona. Abbee  paashistte wotaaddara  generaaletu oosuwa  shocidi  Toophphiya  gooba olanchchata ( arbennata) gita bonchchuwa bonchchees.  I qassikka kaddiyaageeta  wadhdhees( lashes).
Hayle Woldu Sunttaa Teqqa/ Defend The Name/ (1969)  giyaagee haaruwaara( colonialism) oyqetti uttida metota denttees.  Hegeekka ha”i  Toophphiya polotikaassi ayba maadoykka  baynnaagaa. Issi woykko naa”uban   Hayile sillaasa denttikkoppe attin.
Kabbada Ashenafi Paaxettaa (Confession) /1965/ apartheide wogaa woykko   shaakki haariya polotikaa wogaa zaari medhdhanawu keehin lo”o gidiya qalamiyan shaakkiyoogaara  woykko sheeshshan dummayuwaara ( racial descrimation)  gayttiyaagaa. Hagee Toophphiya   awudiyaappe (context) keehin haakkidaagaa. Hegee geelladan Amerkkan(1905)  sheeshshaa ooshshay boottatunne  karettatu giddon  hanidoogaa kare biittan I meezetidoogan sugettidoba giyoogaa.
Kaassata (plays)
 Tewodiroosi G/Medina Tsagaye (Toophphiya xeelliyaagaa. Ethiopian observer 1964 sin.211-228)   giyaagee  Tewodiroosa dendduwaanne kunddettaa layttatu kasiya kaaluwan  A yelaga layttaappe  biidi  A  Maqadala  30 layttaappe guyyiyan goobatetta kunddettaa gakkanaashin de’iyaagaa  zaari medhdhiya  taarikiyaawa  kaassa. 
Oda Oak Orakile/Oracle/( 1965)  kiristtinna gatetussinne( values)  meeze ammano maaratu giddon de’iya dom”ettaa diraamatto meran dumma hanotan qonccissiya doona  taarikiya.  Hagee  issi na’aa  maaretaabaa yootiya keehin  iitiya woykko kokkorssiya hiragaa yara. 
 Yexissiyaagaa /Azimari/( Toophphiya xeelliyaagaa, Ethiopian Observer IX 1964,( sin.229-239)  meeze deretettaa giddon de’iya  arttisttetunne  kushe era oosota  oottiyaageetu bollan  asay dom”etta  hayyuwa oyqqiyoogaa qonccissees. 
Makkala Na’iyo/ The Savage Girl/(1962) keehin mino phalqqettan- Abbe deretettaa harggiya  denttidi bori nashuwaassi –ubbaaba bala  wogetatay ( civilization)  asaa  koyroppe doomidi de’ya lo”obaa, nne  keehin  dosettiya ashketettaa  xayssiiddi de’ees. Gerald ( 1971:365) “Abbe xuma, malaaliya phalqqetta alame hayyuwa keehin dumma gal”a    Amaaraa wogaa  ammanaatuwan   birshshanawu kajjeeliis.” giidi yootees.
Wolddayinnuwa/ Danttuwa/ ( Poetry /Verse)
Tsagaaya (1965) bootta ollattatu Abbay koyro  ba qohuwa gattiyo wodeppe doommidi Afirkkay allaga haaruwaaninne( colonialism) ooratta allaga haaruwan( neocolonialism)  barchchetiis giidi qonccissees.  A polotikaa la’atettay  ikkonomiya kunddissiis. A wogay  atti atti  baanaadaaninne kunddi attanaadan  oottiis. “Karettatettay  ixxas giyoogan, hiyyeesatettaaninne harggiyan erettees. Allaga haaruwa zaari medhdhiyoogan, Tsegaye “Karetta Antigono”/ Black Antigone/, Toophphiya Xeelliyaagaa IX(usuppunne 1965:54)- Afirkkaa bonchchettida  keehin laamotettiya kasebaa  wozanappe dosiya tuussaa Negeretuude  qaaxettaa kessi bessees. I ba cuuccuman hiyyeesatettan, zammaanetettan, Afirkkatettan kumetta biittatetta qofatun un”ettees.
Xaaxi waaxuwan Nuuni Toophphiya bila xiftiya Inggilizettuwan  xeelliyoode, dariya  baggi taarikiyaawa, woganne polotikaa allaltun/ issues/  wudees.
1.Sahile Sellaase Olanchcha Kawuwaanne Tsagaaye Theodroosa amaridaToophphiya  xaafanchchatuugaaranne kare biittatuugaara milatiya ubbaa lagge xeellenna Teodroosa misili bessiya  bila era mooto zaaro.
2.Xuura yarshsho buquraa-  Akisume  wogetaa kunddettaa  beegottida kahaaninne zaari zaaridi  A  beni bonchchuwa qonccissiyaagaa.
3.Yuuqiyuuqennaagaa (Defiance)-  Baggasaara taarikiyaawa  adussa medhdhi xaafo gidiya hanttaara hanotan 1935-1941 gakkanaashin de’iya Naa”antto  Toophphiya Xaaliya olaa bessees, qassikka keehin hombbociya woykko ho’iya   Toophphiya  wogaa ( imattaa bonchchuwaa, goobatettaa) bollan   lo”o hanotan  wudees.
4.Paaxettaa (Confession) – Sunttaa  Teqqa/ Defend The Name / nne Tsagaaye wolddayinnoy/ danttoy/  Karetta aaho deriya  barchchiyan wudidi  Afirkkaa ishatetunne ( brotherhood)   issippetettaa  meruwa shoobbees.
Tammanne Heezzantta Awaa ( The Thirteenth Sun), –Makkala Na’iyo ( The Savage Girl),nne Tama mittaa (The Fire brands),  giyoogeti so giddo haaro allalleta mintti boriyoogaa oyqqoosona.
Aadhdhida 10 layttatuppe habaggan Inggilizettuwan ooratta oosoti attamettidosona.” Gidoppe attin, etappe dariya baggay piroopaaganddan laagettidaagaa.
Map of Afirkkan Literature ( sin.151-152)
1.4. Toophphiya Diyasppora   Inggilizetto Bila xifatiya 
Meeziya-10 
Kaalliya oyshatussi citan gididi zaaruwa immite.
1. Naa”antto Luma Gezo Olaa kaallidi miilooniyan qoodettiya aaho deree Arshsho biittatukko betanaadan oottidabati  aybakko qonccissidi xaafite 
2. Toophphiya betanchchati  Arshsho waanna katamatukko beetiyogaa doommidoy awudekkonne  qonccissidi  xaafite.
Naa”antto Luma Gezo olaanne allaga haaruwa (colonization) kaallidi  miiliyoniyan qoodettiya aaho deree  USA milatiya Arshsho biittatukko seeraa kaallidi gidenna hanotan  lo”o  sintta hidootaa koyyiiddi betidosona.  Hagee darotoo heezzantto alamiya betanchchati bantta biittan de’iya   wotaaddara kawotettatu huqqunna haaruwaappe  kessi ekkanawunne  gaxaappe biidi gidduwa woykko wogga katamata  gakkanawu  shabbirssiya  hiyyeesatettaappe kessi ekkanawu  beetiyaageeta ubbaa gatti oyqqees.
Allaga haaruwaappe simoy sohuwaa yeddiyoogee woykko issi ba koyro sohuwaappe  wolqqan sohuwa yeddiyoogee (Deretettaa,wogaa,ammanuwa,doonaa,issippetettaa gateta,Joogiraapenpne taarikiyaawa moottata) darotoo hanana danddayiyoogee  betiyaappe, allaga haaruwaappe(wotaaddaraa, wogaa, ikkoonoomiya ….h.h.m.),  laamiya ( issipetetta, polotikaa, h.h.m.) , timirttee, h.h.m. qassikka A ayfee  qohettiyaageetu ( victoms) bollan un”uwaa, ba  meezetido wogaa laammiyoogaa, diqaalatettaa,kisaara, yashshaa, melatettaa   h.h.m.  qohota gattees.
Toophphiya betanchchati  arggo ( western ) katamatukko simmidi  betiyoogaa doommidoy 1974   kawuwa aatti yeguwaappe( coup)  simmiina. Kawuwa  aatti yeguwaappe kasiyan  Arggon de’iya Toophphiya asaa qooday  guutta. Hodes (1997)  “ Arggokko betiyo betee  1980yan cora Toophphiya asay 1983-1993 US yiyoogan doommiis. 
USA de’iya daro Toophphiya asay ambba (katama) heeraappe yiidaageeta gidishin  arshshonne arggo  qassikka  Houston giyoosaaninne Dallas giyoosan sohuwa ekkidi de’oosona. Ha Toophphiya asati, “hara betanchcha moottatuugaadankka, hanotatun qohettidaageeta ubbakka   eta bollan oosettiyaabati  eta abbiyaappe keehin  hegeekka daro hanettidabati odettennabanne  hagaa giidi qoppeanna deexxiya  barchche seelanne    kahaa laamerettiya masuntta”Lohhrentz (2004:3).   Hegeetuppe  leemisoti 1970aawa  zo’o/ bootta shabbirssaa, keehin minnida namisaanne dirqqiya,  olaanne wolqqan wottaaddara  haggaazuwa immanaadan oottiyoogaa, hirggaanne  shooro biittatukko dano hanotan betiyoogaa.
USA de’iya Toophphiyaanne Afirkkaa betanchchiti Yitibaarekka Fasilanne Manggistu Dinawu  adussa medhdhi xaafotu  keettaawata  gidiyaageeti  bantta koyro sohuwaappe woykko  bantta so biittaappe laalettidaageeta.  Hagaa gaasuwan,  ba koyro wogaappe, issippetetta gatiyaappe, deretettaappe h.h.milatiyaageetuppe denddaagan laalettiyo( displacement)  qohuwan barchchetidosona.  Eta bollan beettiya laaletta (displacement)  ayfetuppe issoy  melatettaa ( baadotettaa).
Kahaa  bashshiya bollaa masunxxissuwa meezee ba de’o taarikiya  giddon  de’iya  mezeleqiya Nagi mazggabettidoogaadan Beeli Hiyenna / Hyena/( 2001) giyooga giddon  dargge barchcheyo wolqqaa haaruwa, namisaanne dirqqiya,Toophphiya–Somaaliya  olaanne eta  ayfiya yelaga naatu bollan bessees. Hegaa mala oosoy Zinzzotunne Kiitanchchatuppe Of Beetles and Angels: Asegida Maun xaafettida Amerikkaa Ayimuwawu Tumu Taarikiya /A True Story of American Dream (2001). Hagee “Toophphiya /ertera Yelagatubaa yootees. Asegdoma Maui yelagatettan issoy issuwaara olettiyo olaappe (civil war) kessi ekkanawu  ba biittaa yeddiis.  Yaatiyo  gishshawu US   betiis. “ hegaappe simmidi Harbbardde (Harvard)  yunbburshshiyaappe  bonchcho digiriyan ( Ibid:6)  anjjettiis. Haray oyqqiyoobay:  kaali kaalli yiya  eta cenggurssata ( The series In thir own voices)/ 1997/ , hagaassi huuphe yohoy   “Toophphiyaappe baqatiya  Qeeri Na’aa waasuwa”, ;ba garssan   Yelaga Toophphiya Betanchchatu  Taariketa(Stories of young Ethiopia immigirants) naatu maxaafa gidiya  Kurtiziininne Lewisin  xaafettida Toophphiyaappe  baqatidi  US de’iya (Ibid:6-7) betanchcha  keettatubaa yootiya  sooppe haakkiyoogaa( Far away from home)/2000) oyqqees. Qassikka  Yitibaarekka Faasilan xaafettida  Niwu Yorken  Toophphiya betanchchatu de’uwaabaa yootiya   nne Mengistu Dinawun xaafettida  USA giddon zo’o shabbirssaa barchchiyan qohettiyaabatubaa yootiya Saloy tookkido pula yohotubaa /The Beautiful Things That Heaven Bears/ (2007) giyaagaa.
 Diyasppora giddon de’iya Toophphiya asay bila xifatiya oosota leemisuwaassi qommon qonccidaageetu malata  xaafiaa woykko  ayfissidaba gidikkonne, eta oosoti gaxan olettidosona;  qassikka eti  Toophphe giddon bori nashshotuppe  demmana bessiyo  pilliqettaa  wudaa xayidosona. Daro oosoti Toophphiyan baynnaagee geelladan  hegan issibaa  oottana bessiyoobaara gidana danddayees; yohuwan qassi  ha giloobaalayzeeshine ( gilobalization) layttan  hagee aliya atto giyooba giddenna.
Xeetantto layttaappe ha simmin Toophphiya xaafanchchatuppe   yiyoogaa    essidaba  milatiya Inggilizetto adussa  medhdhi  xaafoti Sahile Sellaase  Berhaane-Mariyaama, Worqqu Dayinnaachcha, nne Abbe Gubeynnaan  (1960’s nne 1970’s) doommidi  alamiyan hara baggaara  zaari puttu giidosona.  Keehin erettidaageeti :Nega Mezelleqqiya Wora kanaa Yelida Xoossaa/ The God Who Begot A Jackal/ (2002) Yitibaarekka Faasila Ayimuwa Tekischcheriya /Texture of   Dreams/( 2005)  nne Menggistu Dinawu Saloy tookkido pula yohotubaa /The Beautiful Things That Heaven Bears/ (2007).  Eti USA nne Kanaadan  bila xifatiya woytuwa xoonidi  ekkidoogaadaaninne qassikka daro bila xifatiya xuufetunne ( articles) he biittatun de’iya maxaafaa yigetta oosotu  keettaawata gidiyoogaadan    ha adussa medhdhi xaafoti bantta sheephetuwan de’iyo biittan paaciya aadhdhidosona.  Leemisuwaassi erettida magazeenee, Teqqiyaagaa/Guardian),   giyoogee   Menggistu Dinawu, Teqqiyaagaa  koyro maxaafaa woyituwaara £10,000 woytiis . “[h]  giyoogee geeshsha,  laalettida/ zerzaara/ qofa qashotanne, azzanuwa woykko kayyuwa haaridinne  naageto hanotan”  Mokkiyo  abbiya Saloy tookkido pula yohotubaa /The Beautiful Things That Heaven Bears/(2007)( www.guardian.co.uk., Wednesday,Duubbalaa 5,2007)   giya   A   maxaafaana. Ayimuwa Quxaruwa/Texture of   Dreams/ ( 2005)  giyoogee  US de’iya bori nasshshiyaageetanne  bila xifatiya kaalli xeeliyaageeta giyaagaappe  woytuwa ekkiis.  Toophphiya  -America  on line megazeeniya tadias.com  nne Eleta.com milatiyaageeti  pilliqi yiggiyaageetanne  ha danttouwaaba  yootiya bloogeta( blogs) . Adussa Medhdhi xaafo gidana xaykkonne, Notes  From the Hyenas 	Bels (2001)  kanaadaa kawotettaa generaale  woytuwa   liberary  journal best book of 2001 geetettin  xooniis. Gidoppe attin A attamissida www.amazone.com) giyoogaara  xaafidaagee oona gidana bessii giyoogan  palamay  merettiis
Ha oosoti   kase wode ixettido gishshawu,  Taani  Ayimuwa quxaruwa /Texture of   Dreams/ (2005) nne Saloy tookkido pula yohotubaa /The Beautiful Things That Heaven Bears/ giyaageeta eti waatidi lo”o hanotan Toophphiya diyaspporay  bala qofaappe simmiyo hanotaa wokkalidaakkonne cuccumaa laalettaa woykko paatettaa (thematic analysis) demmanawu   dooraas. 
 Eta oosoti bessiyoogaadan diyaspporan de’iya Toophphiya asati hidootaa qanxxiduwan   barchchetidosona. Oosuwa (job) demmiyoogee  USA de’iya Toophphiya betanchchatusi  gita maachcha,harinne haraashin issi uri qoppido lo”o oosuwawu ( job) haniyaagee. Fasil Yosef, leemisuwaassi, agina kumettaa oosuwa xayidi barchchetiis. Ubbakka NewYorke yeletadi oosuwa xayidoogawu zuuzummiyoogaa siyidoogee I hiidootaa keehin qanxxanaadan oottiis. Taani ta metuwa pude duge yegga qoppiyoogan un”ettays:  Amerkkaa  ooso meezee baynna  ooratta  yiida oosuwa Newu Yorke  ambban  koyyiiddi  de’ida betanchchay  meeziyaara de’iya keehin cora dola Inggilizettuwa haasayiyaageetuura  (native speakers)  annaacettiis (Ayimuwa quxaruwa /Texture of   Dreams/( 2005:41).
 Dola haasayanchchatuura   annaacettanawu   danddayibeenna   haarati US de’iya ooso  xayuwa meeziyan  gayttidosona hagarssara bessidoogaadan:
Daro oosuwa oyttiyaageeti (employers) hara biittaappe yiida magananchchata oosuwa oyttanawu siriyoogaa taani siyaas.  Eti    timirttiyaanne meeziya   xeelliyaagan betanchchati  oychchiyo oyshatu tumatettaa darotoo siroosona.  Eti he biittaa yeleta gidiyaageeta oosuwa oyttanawu koyyoosona; ubba tuma gidiyoogee ammanttenna pattenna timirtte xekkaara  de’iyaageetikka eta guyye qonccidi erettidoogaappe denddaagan oosuwa oyqqoosona( he biitta yeletati) (Ayimuwa quxaruwa /Texture of   Dreams/( 2005:42). 
bantta xalla Hara gaasoy doonaa metuwa. Yoosef hassayiiddi:  “ Daro asay tana duma dumma ooso sohuwaassi qaala oyshaa oyichchidaageeti  ta haasayiyo qaalata akeekidi  taani ooratta medhdhi ekko inggilizettuwa haasayidoogaa be’idosona” /Texture of   Dreams/( 2005:31).  CV waati giigissiyaakko erennaageenne  qaalaa oyshaa waati zaaranawu bessiyaakko erennaagee  hara bana danddayida meto Texture of   Dreams/( 2005:39-44). Yooseefinne hara qaadaara de’iya beetanchchati  ha naa”antto  metuwa birshshanawu  keehatettan- kaafiya  dirggitiya ( Ibid) maduwan he menttuwa birshshanawu loohissuwa ekkidosona. Ha tumu kawushsha gaasuwan Dottoretinne Injjineereti  ziqqa oosuwaara attidi qanxxenna  waayiyaara doosona.
Yosefa milatiya bantta  shemppo xallaa xeellenna   soon yeggi yiido so asaa shemppuwaaka xeelliya betanchchatussi oosuwa xayoy  gita kunddetta.   Eti duretu  gadiyaappe baqatidi, oosoy baynnaageeta gidiyoogaaninne un”uwan  metootiyoogan muleera hidootaa qanxxidosona:
Ta kiisee mela . Ta tanaara ehido   amarida   xeetu doolaareti   wuranawu shiiqi uttidosona. Ha’i   taani  togaassinne kiise miishshaasi  ta laggetun sheephetaydda  de’ays.  Ta oosoy  xayoogan ay keena hidootaa qanxxaakko xoossi erees. Ay oosonne gido. Ha iita gallassatu garssaara   sinttakko tana xeellidi gidiyaagaa qanxxiya issi uray……. ( 31)
Issi  attuma  Toophphiya asi guyye soo biidi oosuwa demmana de’iyaagee,ba heezzu macca dabbotuson sheephetidi de’iyaagee tookkanawu metiisinne Yoseefa keehi yiilloyiis. Qassikka issi gallassi  I  aadhdhido yohuwan qassi I oottanawu bessenna ooso gidiyoogan attida  ooso qaala oyshaappe simmiyoode, A doorettida woykko shiiqida metoy xeeraa gakkiis:
 Ta duuxerettida hidootaa zarbbissaydda, ta  attida gallassaa soon takkana.  Martta tana ufayssana ga baaxetikkonne, qassikka ta  bunchchettiiddi  de’iya  ammanaatuwa maaddanaassi ta olettikkonne, issi deexxiyaabay ta bollan xoppu giis, ta ayyaanaa irxxissidi.  Omarssan ta wozanay keehin deexxin  bolla meecettiyo kifiliya ta bollan  gorddada keehin waassada yeekkaas. Hegaappe guyyiyan taassi guuttaa lo’iis ( 38).
Daro   sha’u   mayleta   kanttida ba duuxerettida biittaappe mal”iya  haattaa googgiya   Mecca  ayimottidi Amerikkaa  yiidi ubba coo de’uwa  bana danddayidi saruwan  de’anawukka oosuwa xayiis.  Qassikka ha I ba de’uwaassi   yiilloityo yiilloy   A  ba yelettido biittan zaari zari yeddetti  aguwa ixxidaagee Amerikkankka ( US) A yeddana danddayibeenna.
 Qaassikka  hiidootaa  qanxxoy  Yooseefa awu ayba miishshinne baynnaagaaranne agina kumettaa  oosuwa oyqqibeennaara gayttidi  A  yeddettiis.   I ubba   oosuwa oyqqida   asaara haasayiiddikka  iita qaaday de’iyo asadan haasayees ha garssaara qonccissidoogaadan: 
Hidootaa xayoy tana urqqa    kessiiddi de’ees.  Qassikka taani yohota walakkaydda de’ays:  bala oosuwaabaassi bala payduwa   xeesiyoogaa woykko   koyroogee nookkin ixxikko naa”anttuwaa xeesiyoogaa. Ta gayttiyo asa  demmiyoode,   co”u  gayiis,   silkke meran taani  malanaassi nookkaas.( 46)
Qaalaa oyshaan wullanaakkonne gi  yayyiyoogeenne  oyqettada  guye caanetta xomoossi simmiya asadan  simmiyaana  giyoogee  Yooseefassi elunchcha  gidiis (49-51) Yoosefi bana qaalaa oyichchiyaageetuuninne xaafetun   qilliicettiis  qassikka  A elunchchatuppe issuwan  ba  qaala oyshaa bala zaariis.(49-50). Qassikka,  I  bana oosuwa koyyiiddi de’ishin qaala oyshaa Amerikkaa gaannatuwan   so biittan oyichchida  betiya  gadaawan oyqettiis(51). Hagee ubbay  keehi xoqqa  daafuraappe, un”ettuwaappenne simmi  simmi yiya metotuppe denddidaagaana.
 Yooseefa milatiya  ba so biittan de’iya issoy issuwaara olettiyo olaappe( civil war) baqati yiida betanchchatussi oosuwa demmido ufayssay hagaa keena giidi yootiyoogaappe xoqqa.  Ha keehin aaro ufayssawu gaasoy I oosuwa xayido  keehin  adussa wodiyawu barchchetidoogaanne qassikka  i demmido oosoy  lo”o qanxxettiya yom”iina  damoozzaa gidiyoogaa(53-54).Gidoppe attin oosuwa oyqqiyoogee USA(Amerikkan) Toophphiyaagaadan  shemppodan xeelettenna.  Qassikka   oosuwa  xayiyaana giyoogee darotoo betanchchata iita hirggissees.  Koyro gallassan I  Inggilizetto asttamaare gididi qaxarettidoogee, A akisenttiya xeelliyaagan imettida  hayyotuuninne  ba oosuwa miiretu sinttan  lo”o tololayuwa xayido (fluency) metoy,Yooseefi banan ammanettiyoogee balbbuqettanaadan oottiis. Qassikka hagee geelladan tana oosuwa xayssanaakkonne  giyoogee  A  qamma ubbaa  xisskkuwa  xayanaadan oottiis(60). Ooosuwa oyqqida woykko oyqqibeenna  Amerikkaa asati  A yiilloyiyoogaa  doommi aggidosona.
Eta kiisee mela gidiyoode  oonikka etakko simmi xeellenna gishshawu,  ha oosuwa  xayaneeshsha giyoogee betanchchati la’an  miishshaa kooshshaadan keessidi de’ennaadan oottiis.(82-83). Hegaa gishshawu oosuwa xayiyoogeenne  oosuwaappe yedetettanaakko giyo yashshaykka hegaadan, harinne haraashin betanchchati  USA (Amerikkaassi) ooratta gididoogee.  Hagee qassi hidootaa qanxxiyoogaa, gita yashshaa, nne Amerkkaa biittaawatettaa ekkiyo qaadaa  xayiyaanaa giyo yashshaw kaalettiis. Hidootaa qanxxoy ( disillusion) betanchchatussi eti sheephetettan de’iyo  biittan  keehin gita waaso. 
Hidootaa qanxxuwa ( disilusuion)  cuccumay ( theme) yaagiyaagaa giddon lo”o dicciis. Huuphe yohoy   ba huuphen   betanchchati   barchchetido  baceesso yiilluwa Uniti statees American ( USA)  bessees.   Danttuwa   yootiyaagaadan haasayettiya   Dantoose   Inferneppe ekettidi  gaannamiyaappe ( hell) gaxi kiyosaara liphida ayfee simmanaashin  saluwa oyqqees.  Hegee betanchchatussi Amerikkan aadhdhida yeemo ayimoy de’iyoogaa bessees.  Amerkkaa woykko ‘Saloy Tookkido Puula Yohotubaa’/ ‘The Beautiful Things that Heaven Bears’/ giyaagee   tumukka puula gidenna. Xeella: ‘Saloy Tookkido Puula Yohotubaa’( USA) giyaagee oyqqiyoobay melatettaa  (emptiness), daro oosuwa,  dagamaa woykko yashshaa (frustration),soo siiqiyoogaa( home sickeness), ufayttennaagaa, bala qifaa(disillusion) , sheeshshatettaa ( racism),   dummayidi shaakkiyoogaa (descrimination) ubbay pula gidenna. Bala qofan gelida betanchchati   yaatin huuphe yohoy USA baaceesso qonccissodan akeekana danddayoosona.  Ha birshshettay ha kaalliya nibaabiyan bessidoogaadan adussa medhdhi xaafuwan hayyottida birshshettaara issimalees: Yooseefi
(Joseph) ba kifile noottiya ha’ikka zaari zaari nabbabiyoogaa doommidaagee Infernoppe  guutta nibaabiya  qaraaridi wottiis. 
Issi irzziizo mala xoo’iyaara beettiyaabaa be’aas,
Saloy tookkido puula  yohotuppe amaridaageeti,
Nu oyddanttuwan yiida, qassikka issitoo daro xoolintteta be’ida 
I uyidi mattottiyo wode, xaafettidabatu giddon hegeeti keehin polo danttuwa/ wolddaynnuwa/ (potery) maara gidiyoogaadan I awaajjana  dosees .” Qoppa hagaabaa,” I  yaagiis. “ Danttee wurssettan siioliyaappe  woykko gaannamiyaappe kiyiis hegeekka I be’iyo saloy tookkido  amarida pula yohota.” Hegee polo,ta niyo yootana.  Co”u giidi polo ( perfect). Ta ta asttamaariyaassi  he maaran  ay asikka Afirkkaadan akeekeennaagaa yootaas gaasoykka hegee nuuni A giddon de’iyoogaa.  Hachchi   hachchi   siiooliya woykko gaannamiya  salo liphetta  xeela kanchchee   A  giddon ( 99-100).
Ha qori kessido nibaabiya giddon de’iya birshshettay hayyottiyoobay Afirkkay gaannamiyan woykko siiooliyan ( hell) de’iyoogaanne  issi keehin qantta wode xallawu ufayssaa woykko saluwa be’ees. Yohuwan qassi Afirkkaa Betanchchatu awudiyan, Eti gaannamiya woykko siiooliya( hell)  Afirkkan olidi  eti yeemottiyo woykko aymottiyo saluwa- Amerikkan de’oosona. Yohuwan qassi Amerikkay eta hidootaa qanxxiyogaa giddo gellissiis( disillusions). Leemisuwaassi, Stepanoossi, ba koyro ooso gallassan  hidootaa qanxxiyogan (disillusions) barchchetiis.
“Aawatettan   ayissiyaage  taani gallassaa doommana koshshees yaatikko  ta aybippe  merettidaakko I be’ana danddayees.” I ta ushachcha qesiya lo”o mahaassi  issitoo  naaqqi simmidi tana sarotanaassi ba kushiya  tawu immiis. Taani A kushiyan de’iya issi issi meqettaa liiqissanaassi  taassi sheneenne  minotettay  de’anaadan  amottidoogaa hassayayiis (141).
Stepaanosi yiillotiis gaasoynne lo”o  oottiya keettaappe yelettidi ayyissiya (proud) Toophpe asadan  I aaro bonchcho hoggi hoggissuwa naagees . Mahettidanne  bayzo ashkkara milatissi pilggiyoogee kwushshiyaaba woykko yeellayiyaaba. Hegaa bollikka I ekkido oosoykka yeellayiyaagaa; suuppa buqurata hooteliyaappe kessiyoogaanne gelissiyoogaa.  Stepanosadan yelagay hegaa haranttuwa efennan ixxidi oosuwa essi aggiis(142).
Toophphiyan issitookka durenne bonchchettida higge eranchchaa Birihaanu takise laaggiyoogaappe keehiya   hara oosuwa demmibeenna.(120) Hagan yiilotidi  Waashinggite ano ambbaa gaxan de’iya  Toophphiya diyaspporay de’iyo apparttaaman Hara asaara darin gayttennan   barkka de’iyo de’uwa dooriis.(120-23)
Jooseepinne Keneezikka hidootaa qanxxiyogaan (disillusionment) barchchetiis. Eti ooratta USA betanchcha gidiyoogaadan etassi ha garssan duutti ekko nibaabiyan be’ana danddayiyoogaadan isstookka   ayimoynne yeemoy de’ees. 
Joseefi he omarssan  ba kolloojje digiriyaanne hegaappe guyyiyan   ba Phd (pi hi diya) Michigane yunbburshshiyaappe ekkanawu halchchuwaa wottiis. 
“Hegee ubbaykka keehin kawushsha.”I yaagiis. “Taassi mereta guuggee woykko eray (talent) de’ees qassikka keehin xoqqa yunbburshsheti koyyiyo mereta guuggee (talent) de’ees.  Ta oottana danddayiyoobaa eti be’iyoodiyan, eti tana ya giidi woossana. Ta hegaan gamma.”
“ Qassikka ayssi Michigane?”Keneeth A oyichchiis.
Jooseefi ba garssa gacuwa qaaciis.
Gaasoykka  hegee keehin xoqqa  ceeggi ekkiya timirtte  keetta. Ta issitoo yaa biida maccaasiyo eraas. A asttamaare. Ta hanno gattanawu gayttido asan lo”o eranchcha (smartest) maccaasa.  A taassi taani guuggiyaara de’iyaaro yaagaasu. ‘Jooseefaa,’Yaagaasu A.  ‘ Neeni  ta hanno gakkanawu gayttido  lo”o eranchcha asatuppe issuwa.’ A taani issi galla  baana gaada taassi yootaasu qassikka hegee taani oottanawu de’iyoogaa gaasu.”
Keneeth, ba baggaara, ingineere digiriyaanne qassikka masttireetiya demmanaanees.” “Ta hegaappe guyye kanchchiyan”I yaagiis, ta guyye Afirkkaa baana yaagiis.” Taani keehin lo”o injjiyan qassikka ubbay, akko xeellana gaana. Hagee  koshshiya asa. Hagee dumma asa. Taani eta xayssiya gimbbiya etassi gimbbana. Etadan ay asinne ayibanne be’enna(146). Tumukka, Keneeth  mulekka I koyyiyo mala injineere gidibeenna. Xeetan qoodettiya A mala qeeri injjineeretuura (engineer) A halaqay wolqqanttiyoogan 12 saatiya issi gallassa garssan oottees. Keneeth he sohuwan wurssayiis gi yiilotidi qaatta oosota (actions), qaalatanne, awu banqatido woykko injetido A halaqaa maayeta hanotaa (style)   ba kase ayimuwa hidootaa qanxxida kajjeeluwan oyqqanawu duuqqees (mimics)/2/. 
Keneeth sitti giidi ba oosuwaappe yees, A kumetta maayuwa kootee guura Udufunee  ho’iyaaba gidikkonne A  bollan uttiyaaggiis. A shamizee kul”iis giyoogaa mala qassikka A karabaatay A qooriya xirphphan minnidi qashettiis.  Hara asa milatennan aggana kajjeeliya   Keneeth Injineere (engeneer).  I wudaa baakko zaaranawunne he assi na’’antto xekkaa geelladan immennaageetu bonchchuwa ekkanawu  lo”o sikettida  kumetta maayuwa  wolqqan ammanees.Ubba saaminttan  I hemettiyo wode issi malabaa gees. I hegaan naaci baynnaagaa erees, yohuwan qassi Amerikkaa asati banqqidoogeeta woykko hanidoogeeta gidiyoogaa ammanees gaasoykka eti issi mala yohuwa zaari zaari goosona (1-2).
“Joseph Kahanga ayimoti kushe kuuchcha keena kaalli kaalli tamaariyo timirttiya (continuing- distance education)   kifiliya   laxafiiddi de’ibeenna.” Giorgge Umbbaa   Eqotaa /George Town Campus (99):  

 I( Jooseepi) Amerikkaa yoosappe   tammanne udufuntta laytta qassikka I he keehin injjetida poo’uwa giddoora  he layttatuppe issuwa issuwa be’ana kajjeeliis. Michigaaneeneenne ( yunbburshshiya sunttaa) PHD giyoobay ha shemppenna yelaga betanchchaa ayimuwaassi cooba woykko guuttaba . 
“Hagaappe guyyiyan Phd giyooba koyyakka,” I taassi  issitoo yaagiis. “Ha alamiyan ne tamaarana koyyiyoobaa ayibakka ha ano ambban neeni la’an  tamaarana danddayaasa.”( 169)

Bantta ayimuwaara dumma gidiya Yoosefinne  Kenneeth zawi bayinna hidootaa
( disillusiment) banttana omarssi omarssi xiskkissanawu ushaa uyoosona.( 145,185). Steppaanoosi,  aawaa hayquwa  dagaman wobbiiddi  qassikka keehin shabbirssiya kahaa laammiya tizitaassi doommanaassi he ayimoti de’okkona. I koyyiyo ubabay buqura keettan de’iya  bankkooniya guyyessan  uttiyoogaanne  co”u giidi nabbabiyoogaa ( 146).  Gidoppe  attin, Amerikkaykka A  yiilloyiis  gaasoykka  ikka assi ufayissaanne A de’uwaassi hanno giyoobaa ( meaning) immana   danddayibeenna.  Hegaa gishshawu  heezzati, bantta tuggaa ( disillushment)   aattanawu uyoosona.  

 Tukke keettatuppe ( bars) issoy heezzu betanchchati  bantta de’uwa kayyuwaa aaro ishaluwan, coo kaa’iyoogaaninne mattoyiya ushshan (alcohol) Amerikkaa malaata wokkaalo qassikka A polettenna ayimuwaa garssaara kessi ekkiyoogaa.(Saloy Tookkido Puula Yohotubaa)/ the beautiful things that heaven bears/.
 
Nuuni heezu skoocheta( ushsha qommo) (scotches) azazida, eta eesuwan uyida, qassikka hara heezzaa azazida . Maccaaasay  daraphaa heezzu daqiiqanne bagga daqiiqaappe guyyiyan guyyiyan    yiidi ta soon  ezgganawu dosiyo 80  pooppe yettaara  simeretti simeretti bagga wozanaara duroosona. Eti durssaa wurssiyo wode, nu xarapheezzaakko sololidi banttana erissidosona.   Eta ubbaassi sunttay Girikenne Roomaa  doona taarikeppe: Venus, Apolooniya, Aprodite – polettibeenna siiquwaanne saluwaabawu qaalaa geliya sunttata. Eti nuussi issibaa imanaappe kasiyan, eta naa”u gellettibeenna issuwa issuwa oyqqidi qassikka Keeneeth  eti ubbaykka puula gidiyoogaadan  etassi yootiis. 
“Puula,” I ba menttershshatun  lallabiiddi yaagiis  ayfee kaaraakko simmidi milatisso  xeela gidiya keehin ufayssiya gallassa ayimo. 

Ushshati tammu doolaare, issoy issoy heezzu durssanchchatuura lagge gidiya heezzu yettatuura wuroosona, hegaa giyoogee  nuuni   issi daqiiqan issi doolaariya  wurssoos.  Qassikka usuppun tammanne hosppun  daqiiqatun  ta he gallassi demmido ubba miishshaa xayssaas( 44-45).
‘Siiqoynne saloy’ heezzu betanchchatussi  doona taarike gididi attiis.Stepaanoos kisaaraappe denddaagaan  ba buqura keettaa xayiis. (67) qassi Jooseefinne Keneeth  bantta issi qommo ooso xallan qashetti attoosona.  Eti keehin xoqqu giida hanotan    bantta garssan haphphido Amerikkaa ayimoti doomettan dummatidi  beettidosona qassikka eti haanida iita tumubaa  ekkidi wurssettan  woppu goosona  qassikka bantta hara de’otu bala qofaa  goshshayoosona. 
Ha heezzu betanchchatu meto hanotay hegeekka hidootaa qanxxissiya ayimuwa, loddan  daganttiya yashshay,nne  bala qofay  daro betanchchatu  bollan erettida zaaretettidaba. Ubbakka ha bantta hoolliya shocidaageetikka, bantta de’iyoosaappe laalettidi betanchchatudan  haahosan olettidosona daro baggi eti koyro amottido woykko ayimottido polo ufayissaa demmokkona.  Eti wullida wolddayinnuwaa woykko danttanchchaa ( poet) Jooseepadan cincca gididi Amerikkay immido guuttabawu A  galatidi  bantta yiilluwaarakka woppu giidosona.  Jooseepi Amerikkaabawu yiillotiya  Estipaanosassi zaariiddi “ Ha biittiya qiiba diqaala na’aa mala. Neeni A neessi koyyiyoobaa immabeykku gaada yiillotana danddayakka….yohuwan qassi A  neekko shiiqa  shiiqa  yiyoode  O sabbananne galatana bessaasa ixxikko A nena hariyaadan guyye simmada saxxana (6-7). 
Hara baggaara, Mesfine Adinew (2012) koyro ontta ( first person point of view), Saloy Tookkido Puula Yohotubaa  giyo ba naa”u lagge Afirkkaa betanchchatuura issippe gididi A de’oy he imatta biittan laaccin mal”iyaagaa gidana mala baaxetiyoobaa yootiya  Toophphiya Diyaspporan  xaafettida  diyasppora bila xifatiyaabaa tobbees, ano eeshshaawaa (protagonist) ,Seeppa Estipaanoosi, tishshenna, ufayttidoogaa banan bessiya eeshshaawa. I  tammanne laappun layttaappe kasiyan Wotaaddarati  A aawaa hayqquwawu matissidi  bukkidoogaa markkati simmidi  Toophphiya xuussaappe (revolution)  baqatiis. I ha’i Waashinggte D.C, Unitide Steetisen qassi ha’i tumu Afirkkaa-Amerikaa hiyyeesatu  shooron de’iya Loogaane yuushuwan   qeeri ushshaa dagayiyo keettaa dooyidi oottiiddi de’ees.  Steepha naa”u xalaala laggeti   Konggoppe ( from Congo) allaga  haaruwa Griillee  Jooseepi (woykko joe) nne Keeniyaappe yiida kase Inggineeree Keneeth . Eti   bantta imatta biittaa issippetettaa misatissanawu eti darotoo issoy issuwaara gayttoosona, issoy issuwa maaddoosona qassikka bantta pudettaanne dugettaa qassikka bantta bala qofata (disillusionments) issoy issuwaara shaakkoosona. Xeelettidoogaadan, etappe heezzati  issuwawu  issuwawu  bantta imatta biittaa meezetanawu bantta  issippe shiiqidi haasayiyo cabbotun issuwawu issuwawu  A  huuphe dumma hayyoy de’ees. Seeppaase de’oy, ba shooruwaara ooratta shoorotu Judithinne bootta maccaasiyo Naomanne ba naa”u sheeshshaappe yelettida assi lagge (siiqo) gidida I na’ee yuussaara laamettiyoogaa doommiis.  Gidoppe attin mataarakka, shooruwa saruwa de’oy Seeppaasa ooratta bootta laggiyookka woykko siiqiyookka hasheyida sheeshsha dom”ettatun (racial incidents) balbbuqettiis. Hagee qassi shooruwaara un”otussinne dom”ettatussi kaalettiis, ba oosuwan yiillotiyoogaa oliyaaggidi ba ooratta laggetuppekka (Judithinne I na’ee Noami) baqatiyoogaa qassikka   kayoyiya   Judithiira de’iya gaytotettaa duuxxiyoogaa. Gallassaappe wurssettan, Seepi   ba suyiqiya (shop) Godaa Yesuus Kirsttoosa Yeletaa gallassan dooyiyo wode banaara baalaa bonchchanawu  so  asaappe ooninne A lanqqen xayin bana barkka demmiis. Taarikkee wurssettawu  yiyoode keehin aduqqi haakkiya A aawaa ishaa keetaakko ba de’uwaassi  haniya shagaxata ekkanawu bees, sinttanay assi ay hananaakko ba metotu bollan phoolissees. Hara guussan, ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy etappe   naa’atunkka  I adussa wodiyawu aggennan koyyio ufayssaa demmennan Steepi naa”u alemetu giddon    barchchetiyo tumatettawu beegottiyoogaa malaatidi kuuyyees. Ha adussa medhdhi xaafuwan   Fasil Yitibaareki  Amerikkan de’iya  Toophphiya betanchchaa taarikiya yootees. Niwu Yorkke  ambbaa  mata  wodiyan yiida  yooseefi, ano eeshshaawaa (protagonist) qassikka koyro ontta ( first person point of view) taarikiya yootees.  Yooseefi wotaaddara kawotettaa kunddettaa (“Dergge” geetettiya) kaallidi Toophphiya quccida 1990 kasiyan  ikkoonoomiyaanne  polotikaa balbbuqettaappe baqatanawu  USA 	 betiis.  Inggilizettuwan koyro digire xallaa oyqqida amarida tamaarisso meeziyan, Yooseefi   wurssettan Raashiyaappe (Rusia) yiida  betanchchata tamaarissiyoogan oosuwa demmanaappe kasiyan amarida hidootaa qanxxissiyaanne yellayiya  aginata  kanttanawu gaddarettiis. He imatta biittaa meezeti meezeti biyoogaadan, I timirttiya go”aa akeekiis harinne haraashin keehin nashettiya diccida digireti ( advanced degeres)  asttamaare gidi oottidoogan A de’uwan injjebay hananaadan woykko A de’uwan  banqqatanaadan  oottido gishshawu.  Hagee I  ba xinaatiya sinttawu efanaadaaninne Inggilizettuwa naa”antto  doonadan tamaarissiyoogan( TESL) Masttireete digiriya  demmiis. Ha injjee ( tamaarisso meeziyan)  I issi aara kifiliyan tamaariyaageetuppe issinneera,  karettanne  bunniya (brown) ayfeti de’iyo qaadadan  attuma laggiya ( boy friend) oyqqana koyyiya  guutta na’ee, Heleeni, siiquwan wullidoogaadan  A de’uwan keehin gita  laame. Heleena aara   koyyiyoogee  dabbotetta  mala gaytotettaa  xalla.  Yaatiyo gishshawu  ashkketettaa karuwa I ippe ekkidogee ekkanawu  assi  keehin meto gidin  hidootaa qanxxuwan, barkkatettaaninne ba aggi yiido biittaa injjiya muleto laamottiyoogan mitettiis. I muletoo ba na’atetta wodiya, ba wodallatettaa,nne cammi-mal”iya Adisaaba yunbburshshiya kamppaasiya guyye tizitaa ba barchchiyaappenne hidootaa qanxxuwaappe sher’i gaanawu guyye hassayiiddi beettees.  Bari huuphiya toohuwaappe la’a kessanawu I keehin lo”o giidi demmido A bizziya,  A bayranne  am”iya  biitta duriyo, godattiyo Hanseno. Qassikka hegaa gishshawu, omarssa wodee ha naa’u bizza shemppotussi eti issibaa haasayanawunne ezgganawu keehin koshshiya wode. Gidoppe attin, Hansoni hassayenna hayqqoy hara sakkiya meeziya A bollan ehiis qassikka bari hosppun laytta mela duussaa Amerikkan  guyye phoolissanawunne qassikka  A sintta ajjuutaa  guyye phoolissuwa ehiis. Hegaappe denddaagan I ba so biittaa ( homeland) guyye bi  xomoosanawu  maachchaakko gakkiis qassikka  ha hanotan  ba kayyoyiya so harggiya zarbbissanawunne  bari qofaa   meran meran shaakkidi  wottanawu.  Gidoppe attin,  imatta  amale saaman, I he biittaa yeddanaanishin, ba beegotaa assi qonccissidanne ha’i A tumu siiquwa guyye zaaranawu maacida  Heleenippe silkkiya xeessay A gakkiis. Taarikee wuriyoodeYooseefi ba sintta de’uwa Heleeniira gidiyoogan keehin wolqqama ufayssan woykko  eenotan   kumiis qassikka so biittan de’iya ba soo asaara  lo”o hanotan zaari walahettiyoogankka  keehin ufayttiis.   A kuuyetta hayyoy: Taani ha’ippe  haa doommin issi saamintta giddon tasoo asaara gidana. Qoodiyoogee  domettiis.  “Taani guyye simmada taassi matanne adhdho gidiya deretettaa giddon gidana…….qassikka hagee wuriyoode, ooni erii ha phikkiya siiqoy geelladan ay ehanaakko.”Ayfe qofaakko yiyoode, ha adussa medhdhi xaafoy injje hanotan keehin daro US betida betanchchatu ubbaassi kotta gidiya daro meezeta  bessees–Amerikkaa Inggilizettuwan haasayiyoogan eti dumma dumma metotun barchchettiyonne tumu keettay anee giyogan haddiriyo metuwan tuggatoosona.

Zaari akeekissuwa
Ha sohuwa woykko awudiya bollan yiida Toophphiya Inggilizetto doonaa bila xifatee, qassikka kayati kayati yiya meto wodetu co’aanne dendduwa kanttidi yiidaagee 1990 aawatu garssan zaari denddi beettiis. Qassikka hegaappe simmin daro Toophphiyaaninne Toophphiyaappe Karen de’iya xaafanchchatun xaafettida  dumma dumma   generetu oosoti  beettiiddi takkidosona.
1960 aawa wurssettaaninne  1970aawaappe kasiyan  Toophphiya bila xifatee inggilizettuwan doommanaassi gaannatonne( diplomatic) taarikiyaawa gaasoti de’oosona. Xaalee Toophphiya woraajji simmin, timirttee aakkanawu ooratta  shemppoy de’ees qassikka Britishe biitta maataawati Toophphiya  timirtte maaratun kelttiya geliyoogaa . Hegee qassi  Inggilizetto doonay naa”antto xekkaa timirtte keettatuuninne Adisaaba/Tungga Yunbburshshiyan  timirtte doona gidiis. Tamaareti bila xifatiya oosuwa Inggilizettuwan  bantta gaazeexan woykko metseetiyan xaafiyoogaa doommidosona  “oduwaanne xeeluwa”/ “News and Views”/ nne bantta gaazeexaa “ issibaa”/something / . Yelaga eanchchati mero xuufiya harinne haraashin danttuwa Toophphiya Heralddiyan xaafiyoogaa qanxxennan sinttawu efidosona. 
Hara baggaara, salo sa’a gufantto nababanchchata gakkanawu koyyiya Toophphiya xaafanchchati adussa medhdhi xaafota xaafiyoogaa doommidosona. Etappe Birhaane Sahile Sillaasemariyama,WorqquDaynnachchanne Gubbaynna Ababa.Hummannatettaa woykko murutatettaa (quality) naagissuwa xeelliyaagaan Dannaachchonne Sahile sillaase  adussa medhdhi xaafoti   doorettida Toophphiya  bila xifatiya oosodan ekettoosona. Harinne haraashin Worqqu Dannaachchu Tammanne Heezzantta Away (The Thirteenth Sun) ubbaappe aadhdhiya  xuufedan xeelettees. Sahile sillaasenne Daynnaachcho oosoti kaalli kaalli xaafettiya  Afirkka xaafanchatu mazggabaa giddo gelidosona. Amarida layttatuppe simmin, Toophphiya Diyaspporaa bila xifatee beettiis. USA de’iya Toophphiya Diyaspporaa bila xifatiya xaafanchchati medhdhi xaafuwaanne yeda xuufe oosota  xaafiiddi takkidosona. Keehin erettida medhdhi xaafuwa oosotuppe, harinne haraashin Yitibareka Faasila  Wozanaa  quxaruwa (Texture of The Heart) nne  Manggisttu Dinnawu  Saloy Tookkido Pula Yohotubaa ( The  Beautiful Things That Heaven Bears)  minttetto woytuwa ekkidosona qassikka  salo sa’an erettidosona.
