ICHCHASHANTTO SHEMPPUWA
5.WOLAYTTA  ATTAMETTIDANNE ATTAMETTIBEENNA  XAAFO BILAA   
Geluwa
Ha shemppuwan darin nuuni wudana bessiyoy attamettidanne attamettibeenna wolaytta xaafo bilatuuna.  Eta wudiyoogeekka  nuuni nu biittaa oosota loytti eridi attidabi de’ikkokka  koyyi demmanawu maaddees. Hegaa gishshawu wolayttan ay hayyo xaafo bilaa oosoti attamettidi kiyidaakkonne qassikka woqqati xaafettidosonashin attamettennan de’iyaakkokka  bessiya wudaa immidi xeellana.
Shemppuwa sintta qofata
Ha shemppuwa tamari simmidi, luxanchchati
?	Wolaytta attamettida woykko attamettibeenna giyo qaalati aybakko  birshshettaa immana
?	Wolaytta attamettidanne attamettibeena  xaafo bilata qonccissana
?	Wolaytta attamettida woykko attamettibeenna xaafo bilaa xaafanchchata qonccissana
?	Wolaytta attamettida woykko attamettibeenna  xaafo bilaa oosotu leemisota  shaakkidi yootana
Meeziya -1
Kaallidi imettida oyshata issippe gidi tobbidi  bessiya zaaruwa immite
1.Attamettida woykko attamettibeenna giishin  woyganawu koyyidaakko qonccissite
____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2.Wolayttan attamettida  xaafo bilaa giyoogeetuppe leemisota immite
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
3.Ane attamettida  xaafo bilaa xaafanchchata  eta sunttaaranne eti xaafidobaara gattidi yootite
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
4.Wolayttan attamettida xaafo bilaapenne qassikka attamettibeennaagaappe  awugee dariyaakko  malan qoppite . yaati simmidi gaasuwaakka yootite
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
5.xaafo bilaa oosoti attamettennaadan oottiyaabati  aybee? Citan tobbite.
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
Wolayttan xaafo bilaa oosoti keehin adussa wodiya qoodissibeennaagee  erettidaagaa.  Hgaappe denddidaagan  ha’i  nu be’iiddi de’iyo shemppuwa hanotaa hiraaganawu  barchcheyees gaada  hirggikke. Wolayttattuwan keehin cora attamettidanne attamettibeenna oosoti de’ennan aggana danddayoosona. Ane ha garssaara imettida  xaafo bilata dumma dumma xeelloos.
5.1. Wolaytta attamettida xaafo bilaa oosota
Wolaytta attamettida  xaafo bilaa ooso giyoogee issi xaafanchchan xaafettida xaafo bilay nabbabiyaageeta gakkana mala geetettidi maxaafata attamiya/darissiya  keettatukko bari oosuwa efiidi kompiyuuteriyan gelissidi he darisso miishshata go’ettidi corayidi giyawu kessiyo hanotaa giyoogaa. He attamissida asi he maxaafaassi  keettaawa/maataawa.appe attin hara asi  a maxaafaa a shenee baynnan darissana woykko corayana danddayenna giyoogaa
Issi attamettiya xaafo bilaa oosoy attamuwaakko gakkanaashin  polettiyaabati de’oosona. Leemisuwaassi issi xifatee kaalli xeelettana bessees. Kaalli xeelettoogaappe simmin A giigissida xaafanchchay A zarettidi wurssetta nabbabuwa oottana koshshees. Hegeekka he wurida oosuwan geellodan gelida bali de’ikko borissennaadan koyettiyo gishshaassa. He maxaafaa giddon issi issi koyettennabi   gelidaba gidikko attamuwawu gelanaappe kasetidi geeyyana bessees giyoogaa. 
Wolayttatto xaafettida xaafo bilaa giyoode issi asi wolayttatto doonaa go’ettidi xaafido xaafo bilaa giyoogaa.   Xaafo bilaa giyoobi aybakko hagaappe kase  nu be’ida. Hegaa maaran wolayttan wolayttatto doonaa go’ettidi  xaafidi attamissiyo xaafo bilaa oosoti darana xaykkonne ane issi issi  leemisota be’oos.
Leemisota, Xoossi immin asi diggenna giya  maxaafaa shoola lenchchi 1975 M.L Wolaytta Sooddon xaafiis. Wolaytta haysiya( wolayta tales) yaagiya maxaafaa  Xaallachcho Geetaachchoy 1998 M.L. Tunggan (Addisaaban) xaafiis.  Hegaadanka Wolayttattuwa  Xon”a Qaalaa Kochchaa Inddiraasa inddaaleenne Milkkiyaasa Bazzaabi 2003 M.L Wolaytta sooddon xaafidosona.  Haranttuwaakka  Wolaytta leemiso haasayaa  giyaagaa  Milkkiyaasa Bezzaabbi 2003 m.l Wolaytta sooddon xaafiis.  Hra qassi kare biitta asa gidiya Sandy Walcoxa & Arina Shortilra Karettida ciishshata yaagiyaagaa 2002 ML Adisaaban  xaafidosona. Tassama de’I Namisettida gaammuwa giya maxaafaa 1996 m.l Wolaytta sooddon xaafiis.   
Ha qommon  xeesettida xaafanchchati he maxaafatu xalaalaa gidennan hara maxaafatakka xaafidoogaa akeekana bessees.
5.2. Wolaytta attamettibeenna  xaafo bilaa oosotanne eta xaafanchchata
Ha oosota giyoogeeti xaafanchchan xaafetti gigidi kompputeriya xaafetti giigidi  attamo keettan daribeennanne hegaappe denddidaagan giyawu shiiqibeenna woykko cora asaassi shiiqibeenna giyoogaa. Wolayttan attamettibeenna xaafo bilati attamettidaageetuppe keehi daro dakkuwan daarosona. Hegaassikka gaaso gidiyaageeti  doomettaa heeran    de’iya shemppotun  nu be’idoogeetu giddon de’ees. Daro xaafanchchati danttota (poetry) nne medhdhi xaafota (fictions)   oyqqidi   ay hiillan attamanawu gattanaakko zooniya timirtte kaaletuwaara yiidi tobbiyo hanotati de’oosona. Leemisuwaassi Wolayttattuwa koyro medhdhi xaafo gidiya Matiyoosa Masppina “De’uwa qumaa” yaagiyaanne “Siiquwa Sabaa” yaagiya medhdhi xaafoti xaafetti takkidosona. Eraadooniyanikka aadhdhidosona. Gidoppe attin   attamissanawu  ha xaafanchchawu gita yeemoy de’ikkonne miishshaa pacaappe aybaappe denddaagan attamissidobi erettenna.Hegaadankka Brunjje Bunggeekka “ Xambbixalluwa” giya huuphe yohuwan xaafetti  takkida medhdhi xaafuwa attamissana danddayibeenna . Haratikka miishshaa pacaa gaasuwan attamettibeenna  xaafo bilati de’oosona. 
Meeziya –2      
Kaalliya oyshatussi gamma zaaruwa citan gididi immite 
1.Wolaytta attamettida xaafo bilaa oosotuppenne eta xaafanchchatuppe amaridaageeta xaafite. 
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
4.Attamettibeenna koyro medhdhi xaafota xaafiday oonakko yoota
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
5.Attamettibeenna xaafo bilati attamettibeennaagawu gaasoy  aybakkonne yootite
._____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
6.Ane   Attamettibeenna xaafo bilaa oosota  qanttan xaafdi qonccissite
___________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________


5.3.Kasetida  Wolaytta  Hayyo Xaafo Bilaa  Xaafanchchatanne Eta Oosota
Geluwa 
Luxanchchatoo,  ha shaahuwan xeellanaagee  kasetida wolayttatto doonaa bilaa( bila xifatiya)  xaafanchchatatanne eta oosota.    Kase   aadhdhida shaahotun   Wolaytta  attamettida  xaafo  bilaanne/ doonaa  bilaanne/ eta   xaafanchchata, wolaytta zamaana timirtte doommido wodiya  haratakka  be’ida.Hageetuuranne  hegeeta milatiyabatu  yuushuwan wolayttatto doonan ay bila xifatiya/ doonaa bilaa oosoti oosettidaakko, odoy ay  bila xifatiya( doonaa bilaa)  oosuwa oottidaakko be’ana.
Sintta qofata 
Ha korssiya wurssi simmidi luxanchchati:
?	Medhdhi Xaafota  gidana danddayiya oosota yootana
?	Chii-medhdhi xaafotu giddon gophphetana( yaratana)  danddayiya  dumma dumma  doonaa bilata woykko bila xifatiya 
?	Medhdhi xaafotanne chi-medhdhi xaafo oosota waayettennan shaakki bessana.
?	Chi-medhdhi xaafo ooso qommonne medhdhi xaafo ooso qommo gidiya oosotu xaafanchchata yootana.
Meeziya  - 3
Kaallidi imettida oyshata   waattan tobbidi  zaaruwa immite
1.Medhdhi xaafotunne chii –medhdhi xaafotu giddon  gophphetana/ziiretana  danddayiya  oosota/maxaafata/ xeesana danddayeetii?
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2..Kasetida Wolayttatto  doonaa  bila xifatiya/doonaa bilaa xaafanchchaa giyogee woygiyogee ? birshshettaa yoota.
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
3.Wolayttatto doonan xaafettida medhdhi xaafuwa hagaappe kase nabbabidetii?
_______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
4.Wolayttatto bila xifatee  ha’i wodiyan ay xekkan de’ees gaada qoppay?
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________  
5.Medhdhi xaafotunne chii- medhdhi xaafotu giddon de’iya  dummatettaa paattada yoota.
______________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
Ha shemppuwan nuuni be’iyoy kasetida wolayttatto doonaa bila xifatiya/ doonaa bilaa  xaafanchchata giyogee  issi bila xifatiya/ doonaa bilaa oosuwan  haratuppe kasetiya wodiyan ootti/xaafi kessidaagaa giyogaa.Woykko issi qommo maxaafaa leemisuwaassi danttuwa maxaafan h.h.m. dumma dumma maxaafatun koyro kochchooro xaafi beettida asa giyogaa. Doonaa bilaa/ bila xifatiya xaafanchcha giyoy  xaafi beettid asa giyogaa. Doonaa bilaa/ bila xifatiya giyobi qassi dumma dumma xaafanchchatun dumma dumma birshshettay imettidoba. Issooti issooti qaala doonaa bila/bila xifatiya giyode  harati qassi doonaa bila xifatiya  woykko doonaa doonaa bilaa goosona. Shaahoti qassi  A gomppaa xunttidi doonaa  bilaa /bila xifatiya goosona. Hara  birshshettaykka qassi “ The total preserved writings belonging to a given language or people.” ( Shipely 1970:183). Hagaa giyogee issi deriya giddon issi doonan xaafettidi xifate meran beettiya ubbi  doonaa bila /bila xifate gidiyogaa Shipeley geetettiya  doonaabaa geetettiya doonaabaa pilggiya eranchchay qonccissees. Haratikka gujjidi yootoosona. Leemisuwaassi ekkiyaaba gidikko wolayttan wolayttattuwa wolayttattuwan birshshiya “Wolayttatto Xon”A Qaalaa Kochchaa” giya koyro wolayttattuwa qaalaa kochchaa attamoy  2003 M.Layttan koyro kochchooro xaafettidi attamuwawu gakkiis. Hegaa giyogee 2003 M. layttaappe kase wolayttan qaalaa kochcha maxaafati  ayibinne de’enna giyogaa gidenna. Hara  maxaafati  Wolayttattuwa  hara doonan birshshidi xaafidosona. Shin Wolayttattuwa Wolayttattuwan  woykko barina barinan birshshiyogan ha Xon”A Qaalaa Kochchaa  maxaafay kasetees giyogaa. Ha koyro koyro kochchooro gidida  Wolayttattoy babaa barinan birshshiyo zammaana maxaafaa xaafidaageeti  Mantta Indiraasa  Indaalanne  Mantta  milkkiyaasa  Bazzaaba. Mantta Indiraasa indaale Wolaytta sooddo yunbburshshiyan  luxissees. Bari naa”antto  digiriyankka 2006 m.l balgguwan wurssidi anjjettiis. Mantta Bazzaabi Wolaytta zooniyan  luxetta  kaaletuwan luxettaa maaraanne luxettaa  miishshatu shiishuwa ano oosuwa polo bussan oottiiddi de’ees. Ha asi Wolayttatto doonaa  dichchanaassi bari buzo oosotakka daro ootti bessidanne wolayttattuwa yuushuwan daro ayfee de’iyo oosota  oottiiddi beettees.
5.3.1   Wolaytta Chii Medhdhi Xaafotanne Eta Xaafanchchata  
Chii medhdhi xaafuwa giyogee   asi baappe medhdhidi, baynnabaa de’anaadan   oottidi bari guugge giddon medhdhi ekkidi yootiyoob gidenna. A sunttaappe nu akeekana danddayiyoogaadan, I baynnasaappe  coo merettidi  xaafettiyaaba  gidenna. A xaafiya asatikka issibaa xeelliyagan de’iya tumatettaa/ hanidaabaa / polettidabaa woykko   geetettidabaa xaafidi shiishshoosona  barippe coo medhdhi kessidi xaafibeennaba. He    xaafiyobay tuma gididi hanidabaa/ polettidabaa giyogaa.  Leemisuwaassi, ekkiyaaba gidikko chii medhdhi xaafo giyogeeti Geeshsha Maxaafaa, Luxetta luxisso hanotaassi giigida maxaafata, issi asa de’o  taarikebaa, haydaabaa/ taarikiya  maxaafata, shiishshi xaafota h.h. milatiyageeta.
 Wolaytta chii medhdhi xaafoy denddiyode Wolaytta haydaabaa yootiya maxaafati, Wolaytta  haydaabaa yootiya maxaafati,  Wolaytta Geeshsha Maxaafati, Wolayttattuwa luxissiyo maxaafati shiishshi xaafotinne de’o taarikiya yootiyabati denddoosona .
Ademsa  Bruusi ( BRUUCE ADAMS) geetettiya biittaawatettay  Kanaada gidido asi Chii- medhdhi xaafo gidida Wolayttatto Geeshsha maxaafaa birshshidi (1995 M.L) laatiniyan qassikka saban koyro wodiyaassi xaafida galatettana bessiya asa. Ha dottoree geeshsha maxaafaa ( Ooratta Maachchaanne Gal”a Maachchaa) xalaala gidennan hara cora guutta guutta ayyaanaamanne ayyaanaama gidenna maxaafata xaafiisinne xaafissiis. Gidoppe   attin dariya bagga oosoti ayyaanaama/ ammanoba gidida oosota.  I hara daro pilggetta oosotakka Wolayttattuwa yuushuwan oottiis. Saaba pitaliya aggidi laatiniyan Wolayttattuwa xaafiyoogee gidiyogaakka pilggiyoogan keehi gita beeraa kaa’iis. 
   Hegeetuppekka leemiso gidana dnddayiyay “ A tagmemic Analysis of  the Wolayta  Language” giyagaanne “ The phono syntax and Morphology of Wolaita Verb and voice system “ yaagiyageeta Awurooppaa asaa qoodan 1983an  attamuwaassi gattiis. 	Ha asi banatettaa yarshshidi keehi adussa wodiyaassi wolaytta biittan xaraphpheezzaa qaale hiwoote woosa keettaa dichchaa ooso keettan de’iis. I wolayttattuwa haasayaakka  luxidi haray attoshin  loohissuwaakka  Wolayttattuwan loohissiis.     I nu he wode haasayiyo   wolayttattuwaakka  yaagokko yaagettees gi giidi  giigissishin be’ettiis. Leemisuwawu   ta  haasayiyoy miza giidi  -miziis-mizissiis- giyoy awudee? Ooni oonaa mizii? Miziyay oonee gi giidi hegaa malabata asay daro go’ettennabata dentti dentti haasayees. Ha mino asi ha’I  mata wodiyan cimido gishshawu bari biitti simmidi biis.  Gidoppe attin keehi gita maaduwa wolayttatto  doonaa bilaa heeran ha’ikka oottiiddi beettees.  Hegaa gishshawu Wolaytta asay keehi galatiyo asatuppe sintta xeeran de’iya asa. Hegaa gishshawu Wolaytta asay  galatiyo asatuppe keehi sintta xeeran de’iya asa.  Aara oottiiddi takkida hara  wolaytta asaykka leemisuwaassi Mantta Tasamma De’ikka unddenna maxaafata Wolayttattuwan xaafiis. Ha oosoti ubbay qassi hachchin de’iya wolayttatto hayyo xaafo bilaassi oottiyo maadoynne kaa’iyo beeray keehin gita. 
5.3.2   Chii- medhdhi xaafuwa  garssan gophphetiyaabata( yaratiyaabata)
Ha chii medhdhi xaafuwa  giddon gophphetana /ziiretana  danddayiya corabati de’ana danddayoosona   Etikka issi hanida woykko haniiddi de’iya woykko hanana de’iya tumatettaa yootiyaabata  ubbaa gidana danddayoosona. Leemisuwaassi- Geeshsha maxaafay, luxetta golliyan naati luxiyo  maxaafati ,pilggettaa oosoti( researches), de’o taarikiya yootiya xifateti ( biographeis) , auto biographies), taarikiya yootiya/ haydaa yootiya maxaafati h.h.m chii medhdhi xaafo qommotuura gophphetiyageeta.
5.3.3 Wolaytta kasetida Chii medhdhi xaafuwa  oosotanne eta xaafanchchata  bessiya zarata

Meeziya-4 
Kaalliya oyshatussi  gamma zaaruwa  imma.
1.	Wolayttatto  doonaa  chii medhdhi xaafuwa xaafanchchatuppe  issi naa”aa gidiyageetu sunttaanne eta oosota  xaafa( oosotu sunttaa) 
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
2.Wolayttatto doonaa chii- medhdhi xaafuwaara paydettiyabatuppe  heezzu leemisuwa xaafite.
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
3.Shoolla  Lencci 1975 ML xaafido  maxaafaa sunttanne attamettido sohuwa xaafa.
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
4.Attamettibeenna  dumma dumma  wolayttatto  maxaaafata  xaafida asatu sunttaa eti xaafido  maxaafaa sunttaraanne layttaara gattidi  xaafite.  
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________
5.Wolayttatto doonan gita beeraa kaa’ida Kare biitta asa sunttaanne I xaafido  maxaafaata layttaara gattidi yootite?
_____________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________

5.3 4.  Wolaytta  qaalaa kochchaa maxaafata 
Wolayttatto  qaalaa kochchaa maxaafatikka chii medhdhi xaafotuura  paydettiya  xaafo ooso.  Wolayttattuwa qaalaa kochchaa maxaafatuppe  attamettidi oosuwan  pee’idaageetuppe denddiyageeti Dooggamo Alemaayoy xaafido Wolayttatto qaalatu Amaaratto birshshettaa immiya maxaafaa. Hara attamettidi oosuwan pee’ida  Wolaytta qaalaa kochchaa maxaafay  Inddiraasa inddaaleenne Milkkiyaasa Bazzaabbi  xaafido qaalaa kochchaa maxaafaa.  Ha maxaafay attamuwawu gakkidoy 2003 M.L  gidishin  ha maxaafaa haraappe dumma oottiyabay I Wolayttatto qaalata Wolayttattuwan birshshiyogaa. Hagaa mala Wolayttattoy bana birshshiyo maxaafati  keehin koshshiyanne aahuwan oosettana bessiya zammaana maxaafa. 
5.3.5.  Haqqaa Maxaafata 
Haqqa giyoogee haysiyaa qan”ishiyanne leemiso haasayata oyqqees. Hageetu  maxaafatikka chii- medhdhi xaafo giyogaa.Ha maxaafata xaafida asati coray de’ana danddayoosona. Ta xeelan kasetees gaada qoppiyogee Shola Lencca leemiso haasayatu  maxaafaa. I xaafetidoy 1975 M layttaana. Ha maxaafaa sunttaykka “ Xoossi imin asi diggenna” yagees.Ha maxaafay bari giddon Wolayttattuwa leemiso  haasayata oyqqees. Ha’I mati 2003 ML Bazzaabbi Milkkiyasikka 2059 leemiso haasayata oyqqida maxaafaa “ Wolaytta leemiso haasayata” giya suntan attamissiis.
Wolaytta haysee( wolaytta tales) yaagiya huuphe yohuwan Xaallachcho geetaachchoykka 1998 ML keehi cora Wolaytta hayseta oyqqida maxaafaa attamissiyogan bari beeraa kaa’iis.Hegaadankka hara asaykka xaafido maxaafati de’oosona.
5.3.6. Wolaytta haydaa yootiya maxaafata
Chii medhdhi xaafotu  qommo gidiya haydaa/taarikiya maxaafati Wolaytta asan gidin hara kare biittaa asan xaafettidaageeti corati de’oosona. Gidoppe attin, etappe dariya baggay Wolayttatto doonan gidennan  hara doonatun xaafettidi beettoosona. Hegaakka tumu oduwan Wolaytta haydaa Wolayttattuwaappe  hara doonaa haasayiya hara asay Wolaytta deriya minotettaa erana bessees giya halchchuwaana.Giyoogaadan Wolayttattuwan xaafikko  Wolaytta asaappe haray nabbabanawu metootiyo gishshaassa. Daroti Inggilizettuwan xaafidosona. Daroti qassikka Amarattuwankka xaafidosona. Leemisuwawu ekkiyaba gidikko Waageesho Waanni( 1990 Ml) “ Ye wolaytta hizib taarik” xaafiis.Amaado Ayshi 2003 ML  Wolaytta Taarikiya Dendduwa yaagiya  huuphe yohuwan  xaafiis. Liisaanu Woldde maariyaami (2003 ml), Gujuubo Asalee 2004 ml , Mootomicchii yaagiyo kare biittaa asi, Fantta panccu, Aaca Iyoobaara keehi aaho Wolaytta haydaa maxafaa 2004 ML xaafidi attamuwawu gattidosona. Hageeti Wolaytta haydaa xaafida  cora xaafanchchatuppe keehi guuttata.  Hara cora asatikka de’oosona. 
5.3.7 Shiishshi xaafotanne asaa de’o taarikiya yootiya maxaafata
Shiishshi xaafoti issi de’iya tumatettaa yaa haa geli ekkidi xaafi shiishshidoba giyogaa.  Hagaa mala shiishshi xaafo maxaafati cora gidana xaykkonne daroti de’oosona.Leemisuwawu “ Karetta Ciishshata” yaagiya huuphe yohuwan maccaasaa qaxxaray gamma gidennaagaa naqaashata yaappe haappe shiishsha ekkada “ SANDY WILLCOXA” nne “ ARIINA SHORTIIRA  giyo boottati( 2002 ML) xaafidosona.
Asaa de’o taarikiya maxaafaa giyogee issi asi bari yelettido wodiyappe doommidi hachchi gakknawu ay heemmidaakk, ay luxidaakko , ay oottidaakkonne h.h.  ubbaa bari gidon oyqqees.
5.3.8. Wolaytta Medhdhi xaafotanne eta xaafanchchata 
Medhdhi xaafoti issi xaafanchchaa guuggiyappe pulttidi kiyiyaaba. Xaafanchchay eeshshaawata bari guuggiyan medhdhidi etawu sunttaa immidi woqaa( wodiyanne qatuwa) immidi tumu alame bolli de’iya asaa eeshshaa immidi medhdhiyoba.Wolayttattuwan medhdhi xaafota koyro kochchooro wodiyaassi xaafiday Matiyoosa Masppina.A medhdhi xaafuwaassi huuphe ohoy  siiquwa bollan wudees. Wolayttan waati labiyakkonne bullachchiya yootees. Ha maxaafay attametti kiyiichchibeennaba gidishin ayyoo 23 shemppoti 150 sinttati de;oosona. A medhdhi xaafuwa huuphe yohoy “ Siiquwa qumaa” yaagiyagaa. Ikka xaafetti wuridoy 2002 M layttaana. Ha yelaga xaafanchchan xaafettida naa”antto medhdhi xaafoy qassi “Siiquwa sabaa “ giyaagaa.Caljjuwa 2005 ML xaafetti wuridi  2006 ML Gifaata aginan 10 saatiyan ha medhdhi xaafuwa naa”antto shemppoy wolayttan de’iya ef emme iraadooniyan  aadhdhiis.Ha medhdhi xaafoykka Wolaytta sabbees,wolayttaa haydaa yootees. A koyro medhdhi xaafoykka Iraaddooniyan hagaappe kasetidi odettidi poletiis. Ha’I naa”anttoykka wuranawu xeeran de’iyaaba milatees. Ha’I mata wode attamuwawu gakkennan aggenna gishshawu hegee polettiyode ane ubbaykka nabbabidi be’ana
Medhdhi xaafuwa masppinappe simmin 2004 ML . “ Xambbixalluwa yaagiya huuphe yohuwan xaafiday xaafanchchaa Brunjje Bungga. Ha’I medhdhi xaafoy keehin aaho gidishin ayyo daro shemppotinne sinttati de’oosona. Ikka wudiyobay Wolaytta dere asaa giddon dumma dumma maabara de’o, ikkoonoome, haydanne wogaa bolli yuuyyees. Hagaappe kase ha maxaafaa xaafanchchay daro yettaata lo’o eeduwan yexxiis. A yettatikka wolaytta haydaa xalla gidennan tohossa Toophphiyan,kumetta Toophphiyaaninne ubba Afrikkaa haruuruwa bolli wudoosona. HA kasetiya yelaga xaafanchchatuugaadankka hara luxida eranchchati duma dumma medhdhi xaafota,diraamata, derssatetakka  xaafanaadan hacchikka minttettoos. Yaatiyo gishshawu  ha hayqqenna xayenna hagaa mala oosuwa oottidi kanttiyoogee nuussi nu deressi keehin lo’o gidiyogaa eridi ubbaykka ane qaaxettoos.
Zaareto oyshata
Kaallidi imettida oyshatussi nerkka  gamma zaaruwa imma
Wolaytta chii-medhdhi xaafo geetettiyageetuppe amaridaageeta xaafa.

Wolayttatto Doonaanne bila xifatiya  T/ Macaraa
Korssiya Qommoy: Wolayttatto doonan Toophphiya bila xifatiya woshettaa
Shaaho paydoy : Wll 428
Wodiya zananay: 3
 Asttamaaree :  M.M 
Korssiya qonccissuwa 
 Wolayttatto doonan Toophphiya bila xifatiya woshettaa giyo korssee Wolayttatto doonan luxiya luxanchchatussi Wolaytta doonaa bilaa/ bila xifatiya guyye dendduwa gidiya taarikiyaanne eta xaafi kessida asatu maaduwa akeekissanaassa. Ha korssiyan luxanchchati Toophphiya bila xifatiya Wolayttatto doonaara gattidi wochchiyogaanikka wudidi  xanna’ana.   Hegaa gishshawu  dumma dumma xaafanchchatun xaafettida dumma dumma maxaafata loytti nabbabidi kase de’iya eraara gattidi aahuwan akeekana bessees. Luxanchchati Toophphiya bila xifatiya xeelliyagan puttu giida dumma dumma xaafanchchata eti xaafido maxaafaa  huuphe yohuwaaranne cuccumaara gattidi shaakkidi erana.qassikka dummatettan wolayttatto bila xifatiyaa /doonaa bilaa xeelliyagankka kasetiya amarida xaafanchchata eti xaafidobas huuphe yohuwaara gattidi shaakkana. Ingglizettonne Amaaratto Toophphiya bila xifatiya xeelliyagan xaafettida dummabata dummabata  loytti wudidi erana.  Ingglizetto Toophphiya bila xifatiya qommota shaakkidi issuwa issuwa  eranaageekka luxanchchatuppe naagettees.
